Important News

Beiping's Preparedness is Serious After Tianjin Incident 66

Traffic Will Be Cut Off After 8:00 PM at Night

The Whole City is Filled With a Desolate and Bleak Atmosphere

Beiping Correspondence: After the Tianjin Incident occurred, Beiping and Tianjin were separated by only a small distance, and rumors also arose accordingly. The military and police authorities, in order to prevent unforeseen circumstances, had to take serious precautions. Although martial law was not formally declared, the state of alert was actually stricter than in the past. Every day after 8:00 PM, traffic in the whole city was cut off. Constitution police stood guard in all important streets and intersections, questioning and investigating passers-by, refusing to let them pass. All shops closed their doors one after another around 7:30 PM. Rickshaws could not be found anywhere after 8:00 PM. The gates of the outer city were closed early at 7:00 PM and opened at 6:00 AM the next morning. Everything was filled with a desolate and bleak atmosphere. Today, the north wind suddenly rose, and the weather turned cold. The sound of the howling wind added to the misery. Because after the alert, this reporter did not know what the situation was like in the city at night, so in the biting north wind, I went to the important streets and markets to take a look at the situation. At 7:20 PM (afternoon), I started from the north entrance of North Xinhua Street at the Central Cinema. There was a row of Big Knife Team soldiers from the Second District, about twelve people, assisting four patrol police officers from the Ninth Section, each carrying a large gun, patrolling back and forth on the road. At that time, the cold wind was piercing and as sharp as a knife on the face. There was no one on the road. All police posts passed along the way were guarded by two police officers standing in double posts, patrolling with guns. When I reached the outside of the Xiwachang entrance inside Hepingmen, I saw a row of security team members in the distance, about twenty people, with a red glass lamp placed on the ground, shining brightly. When the police officers saw someone coming, they shouted "Go back" from a distance. After explaining the reason and persuading them repeatedly, they finally agreed to let me pass. When I arrived at Hepingmen, there were eight police officers guarding it. The iron gate on the eastern side of the gate hole had been closed, and the western iron gate was also partially closed. The police officers firmly refused to let me out of the city, saying that martial law was being imposed early at 6:00 PM this evening and that it was now past 8:00, so no one could pass. The reporter had to explain painstakingly again and again before being allowed to rush out of the city. Passing through the middle of the Glass Factory, the police officers patrolling back and forth were numerous, and fortunately, there was no trouble after interrogation. Then, passing through the Stone Hutong in Hanjiatan, the so-called "Eight Ports" area, which used to be brightly lit, with pipa lanes and bustling traffic, was now desolate and deserted, with few people. Only a single light in front of each small squad was like a bean, decorating the "dead street". The interrogation by the police officers at the posts there was even stricter. Passing through Xizhushikou to Tianqiao, there were police officers standing guard all along the way, and many sandbags were piled up on the side of the road. The former bustling streets of Qianmen Dajie, Shijia Hutong, Dapenglan, and Xianyukou, etc., were now quiet and deserted, with only sandbags and patrolling police officers at the entrances of the alleys. Entering the east gate hole of Zhengyangmen, passing through Dongjiaomin Lane to Chongwenmen Dajie, the deployment of posts by security teams, big knife teams, and bicycle teams, etc., was even stricter. However, what was strange was that Dongjiaomin Lane, within the boundary of the Concession, was still open to traffic, and at the Six Nations Hotel, the sound of the piano was melodious, and the modern men and women were singing and dancing heartily. There were even more foreigners coming and going. Compared with the protected areas outside the boundary, it was truly like a paradise. From Chongwenmen to Dongdan Archway, along Dongchang'an Street, Tiananmen, Xichang'an Street, to Xidan Archway, the security along the way was extremely strict. The crescent moon in the treetops made people feel even more desolate. The Public Security Bureau's bicycle team and the Security Cavalry patrolled back and forth without stopping. Because it was already 10:00 when I got north of Xidan, the police officers firmly refused to let me go, so I had to give up and return. From what this reporter observed, although the security in the south city was strict, the east city was even tighter than the south city. The west city was slightly relaxed south of Xidan, but north of Xidan, such as the area near Shunchengwang Mansion, was also extremely tight. However, among the whole city, those responsible for the security, apart from the police, were all military police, and there was not a single soldier. This was different from previous martial law situations. In addition, hotels and public buildings were all closed at 6:00 PM, and the names of the guests were re-registered in the guest register for inspection.

More orderlies were assigned to duty. In addition to sending gold jewelry to the vault for safekeeping, valuable furs and clothes were also deposited elsewhere. The large restaurants were deserted, and the theaters and cinemas only put on matinee shows. All women's academies and ping academies posted advertisements in front of their doors saying "Business as usual during the day" and "The lamp show will be held on another day." Barbershops and bathhouses drove out customers at 6:00 PM. After 8:00 PM, in the middle of each road, in addition to the armed police officers, there was only the streetlights reflecting the wind and the sound of roaring. (Evening of the 18th)

Establishment of the Pseudo Transportation Committee in Shenyang 67

A dispatch from Beiping states that when the Japanese army initially occupied Liaoning and Jilin, the Japanese government advocated using military force to compel us to resolve various outstanding issues. For example, the preparation to reorganize the local maintenance association into a provincial government was a scheme to establish an entity for negotiation that could be directed and manipulated. Regarding railways, the president of the South Manchuria Railway (Mantetsu), Uchida, and Shigeru Honjo held discussions and, as a result, urged us to restore the Northeast Transportation Committee and resume operations as before, with the condition that Japanese advisors be added. We politely declined, stating that the committee had already moved to Beiping and would be dealt with like other agencies after your country withdrew its troops. The Japanese, seeing no progress, incited Jianxiu Ding and others to organize a separate committee to serve as a counterpart for signing various railway treaties. Ding and his ilk, devoid of conscience, only followed orders. They convened Jin Bi-dong, Duo Kan, and others to discuss the organizational charter and the date of establishment. It was decided to transfer over one million yuan in savings from the committee's accounts in various banks in Shenyang. Simultaneously, Chinese documents and valuables were moved to the Tongze Club, located opposite the old imperial palace. On the first of this month, under the supervision of the Japanese army, they held the so-called establishment ceremony, mutually electing Xiangjian Xiu as chairman and Bi-dong Jin as vice-chairman. The chairman's advisor was originally intended to be Sogawa, a director of Mantetsu, but later changed to Yoshikan Er Usa. They also recruited former staff members, promising generous salaries. It is said that a few staff members went to report for duty, only to find the club heavily guarded. Upon inquiring, they learned that the committee, due to the limited space, had moved to the Sun Gong Ancestral Hall at the eastern end of Jiuwei Road and would only officially begin operations after a reorganization meeting on the fifteenth of this month. Disappointed, they returned. When they reported to the temporary office in Beiping, the deadline of the fifth of this month had already passed. They found themselves in limbo, with nowhere to turn. This serves as a cautionary tale for those who seek to profit from opportunism. The articles of association of the pseudo-Transportation Committee in Shenyang are recorded below: (1) The purpose of this committee is to manage transportation administration matters, in accordance with the original mission of transportation agencies, to improve and connect transportation, enhance convenience for passengers and freight, and increase the benefits of transportation agencies. (2) This committee is a committee-based system composed of representatives from various railways. (Shenhai Railway, Jihai Railway, Jichang Railway, Jitun Railway, Tiantu Railway, Huhai Railway, Qike Railway, Taoang Railway, Taosuo Railway, Sitao Railway) (3) This committee will be located in Fengtian and will have the following staff: one chairman, one vice-chairman, one chairman advisor, and several advisors, counselors, and secretaries. (A) The chairman and vice-chairman shall be elected by the various committee members. However, it is permissible to elect individuals who are not committee members. (B) The chairman advisor, advisors, and counselors shall be selected by the chairman, who will recommend leaders of administrative agencies and organizations related to transportation, as well as individuals skilled in transportation operations. (C) The appointment and dismissal of the chairman advisor must be approved by the committee. (4) The chairman will oversee the affairs of the committee and rule on the proceedings of the committee. (5) The vice-chairman will assist the chairman. In the event of an accident involving the chairman, the vice-chairman will act on his behalf. (6) Advisors will attend committee meetings and provide advice when consulted, or actively express opinions. (7) The chairman advisor will assist the chairman and vice-chairman and manage affairs. (8) Counselors will assist officers and manage committee affairs. (9) This committee will manage administrative matters related to roads, postal services, telephone, telegraph, aviation, rivers, and automobiles, as necessary. (16th)

Pu Yi Intends to Take the Stage as a Puppet 68

But Pu Wei's covert competition is fierce

A dispatch from Beiping states that Pu Yi's plot to usurp the throne has been brewing for a long time. Half a month ago, Beijing sent supervisor Gao Jizong to Tianjin, intending to advise Pu. Because Gao was a Manchu and had previously served in the Ministry of Education during the Qing Dynasty, it was easier for him to offer advice. However, Pu had been planning this for a long time, so Gao returned without success. Simultaneously, Doihara and Jin Liang arrived in Tianjin one after another, inciting him. Zheng Xiaoxu especially advocated for it. Although Chen Baochen and others advocated for stability and did not want their former master to become a Japanese puppet, they saw that Pu's mind was made up and did not dare to openly oppose him. On the evening of the eighth, the Tianjin Incident occurred. On the tenth, Doihara abducted Pu Yi, accompanied only by Zheng Xiaoxu and Zheng's eldest son, Zheng Chui. Zheng Chui was a graduate of Waseda University and had served as Pu's Japanese translator for many years, earning Pu's trust. Rumors that Zheng's second son, Zheng Yu, accompanied them are not accurate. In addition, no other close relatives were informed. Even Pu's wife remained in Tianjin and did not accompany him. After Pu arrived in Shenyang on the fourteenth, the puppet regime was originally scheduled to take the stage on the fifteenth. However, Pu Wei suddenly began vigorous activities, seeking to fulfill his imperial dreams. Because Pu Wei had fled to Qingdao during the Xinhai Revolution, and later traveled east to Japan, he had received Japanese funding for twenty years, leading a dissolute life and befriending many Japanese rōnin. Therefore, in this bizarre drama of restoration actively orchestrated by Japan, many Japanese military men and pro-Japanese factions in the Northeast also supported Pu Wei. In this environment, Pu Wei increasingly felt that it was possible for him to become emperor and intensified his efforts, increasing his plans to exclude Pu Yi. Pu Yi found himself in a dilemma, feeling threatened and apprehensive. However, the Japanese authorities believed that it would be easier to rally support with Pu Yi as emperor, and would not support Pu Wei unless absolutely necessary. They are currently in the process of resolving this situation. Therefore, although Pu Wei is engaged in various maneuvers, he will probably only be a substitute emperor and will not be able to fill the position immediately. (17th)

Establishment of the Jinan Garrison Command 69

Lei Taiping Appointed Commander

A dispatch from Jinan states that the chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, Han Fuju, believing that the current diplomatic tension might cause small people to be incited and take the opportunity to create chaos, has strictly enforced security in Jinan and along the Jiaoji Railway. He also requested that Qingdao Mayor Hu Ruoyu, Jiaoji Railway Committee Chairman Ge Guangting, and Yantai 21st Division Commander Liu Zhennian cooperate to prevent disturbances along the coast. Jinan, being the location of the provincial capital and a hub for Chinese and foreigners, is particularly important. Since the evening before last (17th), security has been tightened. Entertainment venues close early every night, and the streets are cleared starting at 12:00 AM. Pedestrians must answer a password to pass through, and those who appear suspicious are detained. This morning (19th), Han specifically appointed Lei Taiping, commander of the pistol brigade, as the Jinan Garrison Commander. He will be responsible for maintaining Jinan's security, along with Jinan Mayor Wen Chenglie and Provincial Capital Public Security Bureau Chief Wang Kairu. After receiving the appointment, Lei immediately held a meeting at the municipal government. Wen Chenglie, Wang Kairu, Municipal Government Secretary-General Wang Naigou, and others attended. It was decided that the headquarters would be located inside the municipal government. Lei also decided to issue a notice tomorrow (20th) to assume office. The organization of the headquarters will likely consist of a chief of staff under the commander, with Zhao Danpo, the chief of staff of the pistol brigade, serving in that role. The office will be divided into sections for staff, secretary, adjutant, documents, accounting, general affairs, communication, law enforcement, printing, telecommunications, clerks, recorders, messengers, and soldiers. Personnel have also been assigned. It is currently being submitted to the provincial government for approval. The entire pistol brigade, comprising over 4,000 men, is stationed in Jinan, distributed throughout the city and commercial areas. The first battalion of the first regiment is stationed at the provincial government, the second battalion at Nanying, the third battalion at the Civil Affairs Department, the special operations battalion from the West Gate to the Puli Gate, and the transportation battalion west of Weijiu Road. The first battalion of the second regiment is stationed at both ammunition depots, the second battalion at the Jinpu and Jiaoji railway stations and headquarters, and the third battalion patrols the streets. In addition, law enforcement teams and detective teams have been organized, with all of them performing duties. The deployment is exceptionally thorough, and Jinan's security should be assured. Honjo Shigeru Suggests to Southern Army Minister To Seize Manchuria and Mongolia On The Opportunity 70

Taking advantage of the economic depression in Europe and America and China's disunity

Seizing a continental base to counter Soviet Russia in the East and threaten America in the West

Japan's intention to invade, its specific plan, has already been seen in the Tanaka Memorial. We now know that on August 3 of this year, Honjo Shigeru, commander of the Japanese Kwantung Army, wrote to Southern Jiro, the Japanese Minister of the Army, suggesting taking the opportunity to seize Manchuria and Mongolia and threaten the United States. His ambition is even more blatant. It is urgent to translate and record as follows. Reading it, one can know the origin of Japan's reckless invasion of our Northeast.

"To His Excellency Southern Jiro, Minister of the Army, Honjo observes the existence of the empire, and to enrich the status of a first-class country, it is necessary to take the opportunity of the world's financial decline, Russia's unfulfilled five-year plan, and China's unfulfilled unification, to truly occupy Manchuria and Mongolia, which we have been operating for thirty years, and to achieve the purpose of sending troops to Siberia in the eighth year of Taisho, so that the above areas can be integrated with our Korea and the interior, so that the foundation of our empire can be consolidated in the present world. Honjo Shigeru respectfully presents his detailed investigation. The revival of China, the existence of Red Russia, and the American Eastward invasion of the Pacific are all fundamentally incompatible with the basic national policies of our empire. However, in order to prevent the American Eastward invasion, we must first enrich the consolidation of the empire's land defense and the independence of materials. Therefore, before the war with the United States, we must first make the empire's military power occupy a superior position in Russia and China, so that Russia and China will be unable to recover. Even if we cannot completely destroy their power, we can also prevent them from attacking us or having the opportunity to revive in a shorter period of time. Then our empire can obtain a vast and wealthy source of newly occupied land, and use it to enrich the empire's naval defense, to contain American power east of Hawaii, and when the time comes, the Philippines will be managed by us without any problem. Therefore, we can monopolize the western Pacific without anyone being able to compete with us. With American power gone east, British power is in Singapore, and Hong Kong is not enough to worry about us, and will soon be wiped out by our navy, and the South China Sea will also be under our control. In this way, China's four hundred states will be in our grasp, and the unification of all of Asia and the conquest of Europe will not be difficult to achieve. Let's discuss the order of its progress. The first step should be to occupy Manchuria and Mongolia in China and become the country of Manchuria and Mongolia. The second step should be to use the East Qing Railway to attack Siberia and occupy Upper Usk, forcing Red Russia to cede the land east of the Lena River to the Bering Strait to us, and we will assist the White Russians or Buryats to become an independent country in the Far East. Then these two independent countries (referring to Manchuria and Mongolia and the Far East) should be managed by our supervisors. In this way, the Sea of Okhotsk and the Sea of Japan are completely owned by us, and the empire's maritime defense is only on the southeast side. If the above-mentioned territories are under our jurisdiction, their rich reserves will make our empire a first-class country of Jin Tang. Manchuria and Mongolia in China are the three provinces of Fengtian, Jilin, and Heilongjiang, and the easternmost part of Inner and Outer Mongolia, with an area of approximately 740,000 square miles, three times larger than our interior. The land east of the Russian Lena River, namely the post-Baikal region, Yakutsk region, Amur region, coastal region, and North Sakhalin Island, has an area of approximately 300,000 square miles, more than seven times larger than our interior. The total population of the two places is less than 40 million, only half of our total population (including Korea and Taiwan). With such a vast land and only so many people, our empire can use it, and there is no need to worry about the population having no place to consume within two hundred years. Moreover, its agricultural, mining, forestry, animal husbandry, and fishery are so rich that it is impossible to calculate. And its long rivers and huge lakes are even more valuable. Its water power can supply the entire land for power generation, and the Songhua River Plain, Nenjiang River Plain, Liaohe River Plain, and Heilongjiang River coast are all extremely fertile land. With the empire's technology, 30-40% of its agricultural products can make up for the empire's current shortage, and more than 80% can be used for the world market. As for the fisheries in the Sea of Okhotsk, it is one of the three major fish producing areas in the world. With the empire's efforts to develop it, it can obtain more than 10,000 million yuan in benefits every year, and the benefits of whaling are even greater. The horses in Chita and Rehe, and the cattle hides and wool in various places are infinite. We can do without foreign imports of wool woven materials. Petroleum mines have been found in 50 places, and their content is equal to that of Baku and Pennsylvania, so the problem of fuel for our country, as well as the oil for industrial, naval, and aviation purposes, is solved forever. There is a huge amount of gold, and Russia and China have already excavated eight places. At this time of gold shortage, if our empire can make every effort to excavate it, the increase in national wealth can be increased a hundredfold. Coal and iron are self-evident. Compared with the poor situation in our country, it is really like the difference between heaven and earth. If we use it, the future of industry can be limited. The richness of forests can be compared to Canada. If our paper industry uses it, it can run rampant in the world market. If the above-mentioned areas are under our management, within ten years, our empire's wealth can exceed that of the United States. At that time, what country in the world can compete with our empire? With this financial power and this material power, even if we train twice as many land troops as Russia and China, and a navy equal to that of the United Kingdom and the United States, there is no difficulty at all. Then it is not difficult for us to drive the United States east of Hawaii, screen the United Kingdom west of Singapore, and grasp the full hegemony of the western Pacific. The Dutch East Indies, as well as the British territories of Australia and New Zealand, are all in the hands of our empire. Based on this situation, we can advance to conquer the entire territory of China, as well as all of Asia, and then conquer all of Europe and Africa, and grasp the land of the eastern hemisphere, to share the world equally with the United States. This is the legacy of our Emperor Meiji, and the responsibility that our Yamato nation should have. At this time, Russia and China are still in the preparation stage of revival, and their strength is weak. If we meet them with a strong land army, it will be like destroying withered and rotten things. If we miss this opportunity and do not plan, and sit and wait for China's unification to be completed, Chiang Kai-shek's ambition to revive China will be achieved, and the Red Russia's five-year plan will be completed, not only will the hopes for the empire's future become a bubble, but the empire's great disaster will be imminent. I hereby submit the findings of the investigation and detailed illustrations for your attention. (Illustrations omitted)

Jin Yudong Handles Affairs According to Japanese Intentions

A dispatch from Harbin states that after Xi Qia, under the command of the Japanese, appointed Jin Yudong, a mixed-race person, as the director of the Jichang and Jidun Railways, all section chiefs and section heads above the level in the bureau were replaced by Japanese. Jin also considered himself a Japanese, so the policy direction did not await Xi Qia's instructions, but directly consulted Mantetsu. The Jidun and Jichang Railways were not connected, but after the Japanese forcibly connected the Jihai Railway, the Jidun and Jichang Railways also implemented the connection on the 14th of this month. Jin's request to Xi Qia was for reducing expenses and making management easier. The Japanese had already agreed to it in advance, and Xi Qia naturally did not dare to reject it afterwards. As a result, the three Jilin railways (Jichang, Jihai, Jidun) have completed a line. Jin also recruited scattered soldiers and defeated Yong to form a railway protection security team with 7,000 people, and concurrently served as commander. The reorganization charter of the bureau after the merger of the two railways, as stipulated by Jin Yudong, is recorded below: (Article 1) The Jichang and Jidun Railways manage the railway from Changchun to Dunhua. (Article 2) The Jichang and Jidun Railway Administration manages the matters stipulated in Article 2 of the National Railway Organization and Compilation Week. (Article 3) The Jichang and Jidun Railway Bureau has the following departments: (1) General Affairs Department, (2) Transportation Department (3) Engineering Department, (4) Accounting Department, (5) Police Department, (Article 4) The General Affairs Department is responsible for various matters in accordance with the following regulations: The Document Section is responsible for the receipt and dispatch of documents, the promotion and demotion and rewards and punishments of employees, and the custody of archives and seals, handling academic affairs, investigating the business status of the entire railway, compiling reports, and other confidential matters. The Audit Section is responsible for reviewing engineering plans, material prices, supervising the purchase of engineering and land, and examining various evidentiary documents, receipts and disbursements of money, budgets and settlements, and all matters related to contracting. (Article 5) The Transportation Department is responsible for various presentations in accordance with the following regulations: The Affairs Section is responsible for transportation-related documents and personnel, as well as reviewing business income, registering accounts, compiling registers and statistics, monitoring ancillary business expenses, and other general affairs. The Car Affairs Section is responsible for the business of the road and ancillary businesses, as well as business accidents, intermodal transport and train operation, safety signals, distribution of passengers and goods, and electrical communications. The Machinery Section is responsible for the custody of vehicles, machinery, and equipment, and their repair plans, as well as the supervision of vehicle operation, the review of operation accidents, the investigation of transport and machinery materials, the statistics of vehicles and machinery, and the allocation of locomotive coal and water. The Car Affairs General Section directs and supervises the heads of the various car affairs sections. The Changchun Factory is responsible for the design of vehicles and machinery, as well as manufacturing, repairing and inspecting transportation and machinery materials. The Car Affairs Section is responsible for all car affairs matters within the section. The Machinery Section is responsible for all machinery matters within the section. The Station is responsible for all matters within the station. (Article 6) The Engineering Department is responsible for various matters in accordance with the following regulations: The Affairs Section is responsible for engineering-related documents and personnel, as well as contracting projects, engineering materials, and other general affairs. The Engineering Section is responsible for the planning, construction, maintenance, and preservation of land, lines, and buildings, as well as all electrical equipment. The Engineering Section is responsible for all engineering matters within the section. (Article 7) The Accounting Department is responsible for various matters in accordance with the following regulations: The Accounting Section is responsible for accounting-related documents and personnel, compiling accounting statistics and budgets for calculations, and the receipt, disbursement, and custody of money and securities, as well as other general affairs. The Expenditure Section is responsible for the purchase, distribution, and disposal of materials and goods. The Warehouse is responsible for the inspection, receipt, dispatch, and custody of materials and goods (Article 8) The Police Department is responsible for various matters in accordance with the following regulations: The Affairs Section is responsible for police-related documents and personnel, as well as public health, medical affairs, and other general affairs. The Police Section is responsible for the compilation and administration of all railway police, the implementation of railway boundary security, and the command of various police subsections and outposts, handling security affairs, and fire prevention matters. Section heads, factory directors, section chiefs, station heads, and warehouse directors. (Article 9) The Bureau has a secretary who handles the confidential translations of the director and company representatives and other matters not belonging to the department. (Article 10) The quota of management staff of the Jichang and Jidun Railways is in accordance with the attached table. (Article 11) The Jichang and Jidun Railway Administration is responsible for all matters under the jurisdiction of this Bureau.

Songjiang 72

The Fourteenth District Opposes Changing County Jurisdiction Fengxian County proposed that Caojing, Huan'an, Que, Hujiaqiao, Zhalin, and other places east of the Yepu Pond in Punan, and north of the Longquan Port, be placed under the jurisdiction of Fengxian, and requested the Civil Affairs Department to transfer the matter to Mu County for review and reply. After the transfer to the relevant 14th and 15th districts of the above-mentioned areas, local people were convened to discuss and reply in detail. It is now known that Gu Wen, the head of the 14th district, convened a meeting on the 20th after receiving the order to solicit the opinions of the entire district. They all believed that the proposed annexation of the eastern section of the Yepu Pond River by Fengxian County, and the transfer of jurisdiction, was inconsistent with the provisions of Article 3, Item 1 of the Outline of the Administrative Regional Arrangement of Fengxian County. According to the natural boundary between the district and Fengxian, the Qianbu Jing River, the boundary line is clear and there is no need to change it. The proposal to transfer the eastern section of the Yepu Pond River under jurisdiction was considered to have no reason and was difficult to recognize. It was decided to pass this resolution and submit it to the county government for review. According to the change of county jurisdiction, the relationship is more than just the two districts, so it is appropriate to collect the opinions of the entire county conference and protest on the basis of reason, so as to avoid disputes. Wuxi 74

Issues in the Trial of Cases by Temporary Courts The president of the High Court, Lin Biao, formerly used the cases tried by the temporary courts organized by various counties in accordance with the Emergency Crime Law to Endanger the Republic of China. According to Article 8, Paragraph 1 and Paragraph 2 of the law, those who should be sent to this court for review are specifically for guilty verdicts. If the verdict is innocent, dismissed, not accepted, or the jurisdiction is incorrect, should it be submitted to this court for review? In another case, part of the verdict was guilty and part was innocent, dismissed, or not accepted. Once submitted, in addition to the guilty part being reviewed, should the remaining parts be reviewed together? The law does not have clear provisions on how to handle the matter. The matter has been submitted to the Ministry of Justice for instructions. It is now informed by the ministry's reply that the approval procedure stipulated in Article 8 of the Emergency Crime Law to Endanger the Republic of China is specifically for when the verdict is guilty. The provisions are clear and have been submitted to the Judicial Yuan for instructions and compliance. In a case where part of the verdict is guilty, a corresponding solution can be obtained. Yesterday, Chen County magistrate was specially instructed to know this.

Frequent Robbery Cases in the Countryside The house of Hua Jinshan, a villager from Huajiaqiao Township, Xin'an District, District 13 of the county, suddenly came to twelve bandits around 10 p.m. the night before last. They broke into the house, held pistols to intimidate, and searched wantonly, robbing clothes, jewelry, and single deeds. The loss was not small. The bandits were still not satisfied and went to the house of Hua Yanhu next door to rob. Unexpectedly, the valuables had already been hidden, and only more than ten yuan of silver and a few pieces of cloth were found. They carried the loot and went towards the station. The two families lost about 700-800 yuan. In the Yangjiaocao area outside the East Gate, the house of Xie Rongquan, a villager, was visited by seven or eight bandits the night before last. They broke into the house, and Xie heard the alarm and rushed out of the back door and called out to warn. The bandits knew they were prepared and fled. Delegation Meeting of University Students Going to Beijing to Urge the Government to Send Troops 79

| Three Demands Resolved |

| Vow to Not Return Until Goals Are Achieved |

| Meeting to Continue at 1 PM Today, Departing Tomorrow |

The representatives' assembly of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Federation of university students in this city resolved that a delegation of representatives freely formed by each school would go to Beijing on the 23rd of this month to urge the government to send troops. It is learned that the delegation held a meeting from 7:00 PM to 10:00 PM yesterday at the Youth Propaganda Corps. Representatives from over ten schools, including Fudan, Jiaotong University, Guanghua, Shanghai, Liangjiang Merchant Marine, Chinese, Specialties, French Medical, Chinese Medicine Specialty School, Shanghai Art Specialty School, and Xinhua, attended. Zhou Xiaobo of Fudan was elected as chairman, and Pan Chuji was the recorder. The chairman reported that because of the rush of Saturday, some schools had not yet finished collecting volunteers to go to Beijing, and therefore, representatives had not yet been dispatched. Subsequently, the following important resolutions were passed: (1) The goals of going to Beijing: For the Fourth National Congress, the request is for the congress to resolve the matter on the spot. If Chairman Chiang does not comply with the instruction to personally lead troops to recover lost territory within the time limit set by Chairman Chiang at the Fourth National Congress, then he must be expelled from the party. For the National Government, the requests are: (1) Request Chairman Chiang to personally write a pledge in public, specifying (1) the latest date of departure and (2) a statement that he will not return to Nanjing until the lost territory is recovered. (2) Request the government to order Zhang Xueliang to immediately send troops to recover the lost territory. If there is no indication of troop deployment within three days, he will be dismissed and severely punished. If the above three demands are not satisfactorily answered, the entire group will gather at the Fourth National Congress venue or in front of the National Government, regardless of day or night, wind or rain, and will not disperse. If the answer is satisfactory, they will immediately return to Shanghai. (2) Each person will fill out a pledge, stating: "In accordance with the resolution of the Student Federation, with boiling blood and the greatest determination, I voluntarily go to Beijing to urge the government to send troops. I vow not to return alive until the goals are achieved. This I, [Name], solemnly swear." (3) Organizational and disciplinary issues will be finalized at the second delegation meeting at 1:00 PM today (the 22nd). (4) Registration for each school will close today. (5) Please have the Student Federation intensify the work of classmates in the rear. (6) The Student Federation will issue general flags and badges. Regarding transportation, if the Railway Bureau refuses to issue tickets, it is said that the delegation going to Beijing will lie down on the railway tracks between Nanjing and Shanghai. Regarding funding, each person will only bring expenses for travel from their school to the train station. After arriving in Beijing, accommodation will be at the Fourth National Congress venue or outside the National Government gate. Regarding food, most people advocate requesting the government to provide it. A minority advocates fasting until a satisfactory result is achieved. No final decision has been made.

Shi Gude Was Extremely Dominant 87

In yesterday's big battle, Shi Gude had the upper hand throughout. In the first half, they dominated the field and were invincible. Donghua was under pressure throughout. In the second half, Donghua gradually gained momentum, but unfortunately, they failed by a narrow margin. Towards the end, due to the impulsive actions of the audience, the order was fortunately not disrupted. Both sides were also fierce, and several people were injured. In terms of performance, Shi Gude was indeed superior. Their coordination was pure and fiery, and their attacks were powerful. Since the ball was mostly at the feet of the British army, their victory was not accidental.

Donghua Team's Second Crisis 88

After the crisis passed, they thought the worst was over, but who knew that the result would still be a loss. Xi Qiaosheng attacked the goal three times, but all were just short. Shi Gude then returned with a vengeance. Duran invaded along the right side. Chen Pu caught up, Duran avoided the obstacle, and fired a long shot, reaching the right side. Williams passed the wing, and Dai caught the ball and attacked the goal. Although Zhou Xianyan caught the ball, he couldn't kick it out immediately. Pan Erden had already rushed in, encircling the goal. Zhou Xianyan then rushed out of the goal, having abandoned the ball. But it had already reached the penalty line, so he couldn't use his hands. Luofande intercepted the ball and shot it into the empty goal, hitting the side post and going in. Donghua then lost its defense.

The Loss Due to the Goalkeeper Rushing Out 89

After the crisis passed, we thought the worst was over, but who knew that the result would still be a loss. Xi Qiaosheng attacked the goal three times, but all were just short. Shi Gude then returned with a vengeance. Duran invaded along the right side, Chen Pu caught up, Duran avoided the obstacle, and fired a long shot, reaching the right side. Williams passed the wing, and Dai caught the ball and attacked the goal. Although Zhou Xianyan caught the ball, he couldn't kick it out immediately. Pan Erden had already rushed in, encircling the goal. Zhou Xianyan then rushed out of the goal, having abandoned the ball. Since it had already reached the penalty line, he couldn't use his hands. Luofande intercepted the ball and shot it into the empty goal, hitting the side post and going in. Donghua then lost its defense.

Hoping to Lose One Less Goal 90

Donghua tried hard to counterattack, and Dai Linjing worked hard to charge the goal, but failed to enter. Chen Yutian shot from afar, but lacked power. Qian Jingyong bravely stepped forward, but was blocked by Gray. Chen Yutian attacked forward again, but was kicked out by Hamilton. Missing several opportunities, dangerous situations appeared again. Pan Erden and Duran came together. Duran ran to the front of the goal and shot directly. Zhou Xianyan rushed up again and kicked it out. Pan Erden received the ball on the right, quickly passed it to the center, Lovander dodged the incoming person, passed it to the left again, and Williams shot again. Zhou Xianyan was still outside the goal, and the goal was lost again. Before long, the first half ended.

Blaming Only Their Own Bad Luck 91

In the second half, Donghua gradually showed a turning trend, not as heavily pressed as in the first half. However, back and forth, neither side achieved any results. After most of the half had passed, the audience saw Xi Qiaosheng attacking the goal, and Hamilton bumped into him from the side, causing him to miss. This happened twice, causing a great uproar. According to the rules of the game, there is such a thing as a legal collision. The resulting dispute almost became unmanageable. Thus, both sides became increasingly intense due to the agitation of the audience. Zhou Xianyan and Hamilton were injured one after another, and Neil was sent off. The fierce battle ended in this way. I think that viewers should not blame the referee or others, but rather blame their own bad luck with the ball.

Minutes of the Meeting of the Chinese Football Association Committee 97

The Chinese Football Association Committee held a meeting at the Jinling Restaurant the night before last. The committee members present were Le Xiurong (Chairman), Feng Jianwei, Ma Detai, Shen Kunnan, Shen Guoquan, and Zhou Jiaqi (Secretary). They discussed various matters related to the association. The meeting lasted for three hours before adjourning. The resolutions passed are excerpted below:

(1) The request of the Yiyong Team to change its name to "Yiyong" was approved.

(2) Regarding the assault that occurred during the Yong'an vs. Postal Service match on November 8th, according to the report of the referee of the match and the investigation of the facts, it was initiated by the linesman sent by Yong'an who entered the field and used force. It was found that the linesman, in his position as a match official, started the fight, which was an absurd act. Since the linesman was sent by the Yong'an team, the team cannot escape blame for his incompetence. It was resolved to permanently revoke the qualifications of the linesman, Ruan Xiuzhang, to participate in matches, represent the Chinese Football Association, or hold any position within the association. In addition, a formal letter of warning should be sent to the team, urging them to conduct themselves properly and not repeat the same mistake, in order to maintain the spirit of the association. As for the match itself, since the captains of both teams stated to the referee at the time that they were unwilling to continue the match in order to avoid danger, and since the incident occurred outside of the players, the match was suspended. The Referee Committee and this committee both agreed that the match should be rescheduled.

Free Talk

Voice of Resistance Against Japan

Feeling After Ma Zhanshan's Isolated Army Exhausted Their Strength and the City Fell 99

— Liang Yangong

The sound of killing enemies is hoarse, strength is exhausted. The shattered land and rivers are unbearable to look back upon. Weaver Girl smashes the good home. A single tree trunk is difficult to support the great mansion. Brave men spit out only hot blood, husbands repay the country relying on loyal hearts. Gentlemen fold their hands, the common people are misled. Eternal sorrow lies in cowardly peace. Yagong, a Xiaolian, has been reading in seclusion in Shanghai in recent years, unaware of the chaos. Comparing this to the daily urgency of national disasters, he is filled with sorrow. Recently, he heard that General Ma had exhausted his strength and retreated. He was moved and immediately drafted a poem to express his feelings. Yagong is over seventy years old, but his concern for national affairs does not yield to the vigorous youth. This poem is specially recorded and submitted to Free Talk for public viewing. Zou Yifei adds a note.

Four Old Women Resisting Japan and Saving the Country 100

— Cold Cicada

In the sound of national crisis, the enthusiasm of young people to resist the enemy is self-evident. Even the products of sixty or seventy years ago, the decrepit old women of modern China, are also passionate and fully express their spirit of resisting Japan and saving the country. This is indeed something that we can take as a bit of comfort amidst extreme grief and indignation. I am eager to record it and tell the people of the country.

Beijing, October 2nd dispatch. Zhang Zongchang's mother recently arrived here from Dalian. She expressed to people that Xiaokun (ie Zongchang) must never be a slave to the country. I cannot teach him to do things that humiliate the country either. He will come to Ping in the next few days. If there is any act of selling the country, I will commit suicide to thank the people of the country.

Nanchang, October 2nd dispatch. Recently, an old woman shouted "Down with the Japanese invaders!" and threw herself into the Zhang River to commit suicide.

Nanjing, October 5th dispatch. Personnel from the Liaoning Court came to Beijing to report that Zang Shiyi is still being monitored by the violent Japanese. The Japanese army ordered him to sign. Zang refused and cried loudly, saying that his old mother was seventy years old and wanted to see her one last time before he died. The Japanese officer sent his mother to the South Manchurian Railway Station. They ordered a meeting, and ordered the mother to persuade Zang. The mother said, "Since ancient times, when a city falls, it falls completely. You must die rather than sign." The Japanese army then sent her away.

Harbin, November 3rd dispatch. Zhang Zuoxiang's guard, Feng Zhanhai's regiment, withdrew from the provincial capital when the Japanese army entered Jilin. It was the most complete retreat among the Jilin army. The Japanese military police headquarters in Jilin arrested Feng Zhanhai's mother-in-law, Song, and forced her to ask about the direction of Feng's retreat, and ordered her to lure Feng. Song refused, was beaten and almost died, and then was released.

Cold Cicada says. The word "death" in the dictionary is the most ominous term. People avoid talking about it, especially women. Today, Song would rather die than submit. An old woman in Nanchang encouraged the people of the country with her death. Zang's mother taught her son to die rather than sign. Zhang's mother guaranteed her son's non-traitorous behavior with her death. Every word of "death" is like a drop of blood. Among them, Zang's mother's few words are particularly strict in wording, decisive, and the intention is painful, turning around a hundred times. Hoping that the mountains and rivers will be restored after being broken. Teaching her son to seek life from death. The words are earnest, making people hear and feel sad. Alas, if women are still like this, what about men? If old people are still like this, what about young people? Shouldn't our patriotic youth, our patriotic men, work harder?

The National Salvation Movement of the Women's World 101

— Sun Choucheng

The Shanghai Women's National Salvation Grand Alliance held a memorial service on the fifth floor of the Shanghai Women's Bank on the 20th of this month to comfort the flood victims and the compatriots in the Northeast. The tragic situation is difficult to describe in words. I hereby record one or two to inform all sectors.

The layout of the venue was different from usual. The four characters "Spirits Never Die" were hung high as a vertical scroll to replace the spirit tablet. Beside it were couplets that read "Protect our rivers and mountains, glorify our nation, and lead us only by the martyrs." "Repel the crazy bandits, kill the Japanese slaves, and who will continue the fight." This was offered by the Liangjiang Women's School. Three bottles of fresh flowers were placed on the table, without sacrificial dishes, incense, or candles. Xu Renyi read the will of the Prime Minister. Yang Xizhen offered flowers to the dead compatriots and bowed in silent mourning. Mao Wang Ruizhu reported the purpose of the meeting, detailing the tragic situation of the floods in various provinces and the brutal acts of the Japanese in forcibly occupying the Northeast, which made people unable to bear to hear it. Huang Shaolan read the eulogy, which was thousands of words long. There were painful words such as "How could it be that disaster suddenly arises within the walls, burning the beans with the stalks, and the pond fish suffer. The blood and fat are sprinkled on the plains, and the livers and brains are smeared on the ground. Hundreds, thousands, even billions, are injured or killed. It is sad to die physically, but it is even more painful to die mentally." The entire venue was solemn, and some even shed tears. Dozens of elegiac couplets were hung on the four walls, which cannot all be mentioned. I will record one or two from memory as follows. "The leopard skin still exists, and we are extremely angry. Sometimes we write to the government, sometimes we telegraph all parties. We must restore the territory of the Republic of China to the outside world. Longcheng is lost, and we hope that everyone will rise up to save the country. Either donate money or wear armor and wield weapons, and help General Ma together." "You all competed to take the lead in suppressing the rebellion and defending against insults. Remembering the heroic name in history, it will always remain a model. We are willing to be the successors in taking righteousness and achieving benevolence. It is the season of yellow flowers, and we jointly comfort the loyal souls." "All the comrades fought desperately to save the country, only hoping that someone will continue the fight. How many heads of the wooden clogs? Our women are summoning souls to establish the country. We only hope that the hearts of the people will not die, and take the means of Kublai Khan to come again." Li Guanfang said that the Republic of China takes the people as the masters, so the status of our women is equal to that of the empresses and princesses of the empire. We must recognize national affairs as our own affairs. In the past twenty years, this is the first time we have fought a war against foreign countries. Unfortunately, we failed. How bad is the harm? Soldiers must have the determination to die. We should sell our jewelry to help with military expenses. Huang Shaolan said that a country must be attacked from within before it is attacked by others. This external disaster was caused by internal strife. The National Government is different from the warlord era. Since the words "National" are crowned above the government, then all citizens, regardless of gender, should unite in the face of the disaster, the autumn of survival and urgency, and request the government to unite as soon as possible and unanimously deal with foreign countries. Therefore, our association has drafted a telegram today, asking the ladies of the Legislative Yuan, Song Meiling, Song Ailing, and Zhang Mojun, to present it to the government as soon as possible to send troops to rescue the Northeast and drive the Japanese slaves out of the country in order to consolidate national defense. If you agree with this, please raise your hands. Hundreds of jade arms were raised at the same time, and Camellia assumed the responsibility, all saying that the hearts of the people have not died, and the country can still be saved. Therefore, the telegram was drafted and sent according to the plan.

A Record of Zhang Gan, Who Severed His Finger to Swear an Oath 102

— Reason

Zhang Gan, a student of the Southeastern Medical College in this city, severed his finger yesterday to write an oath in blood, which caused a sensation near Nanshi. Mr. Zhang disregarded everything and severed his finger to show his determination. His ambition is commendable, and his situation is pitiful. Therefore, the beginning and end of the matter are recorded.

Organizing a Support Black Rescue Team The students of the school, in view of General Ma Zhanshan's isolated army fighting to the death with the Japanese army in the remote frontier, with their thin clouds in the sky, making contributions to the country, in order to increase his strength, specially organized a support Ink rescue team. More than 100 people signed up to participate at one time, and many of them were senior classmates with rich knowledge. The leader of the team, Zhang Gan, saw the situation and said that he was preparing to go to Heilongjiang and raise funds for medicines.

Difficulties Abound This time, the team leader notified all team members to sell all their belongings and books to pay for the journey. The team members were embarrassed, and many of them withdrew. As a result, only more than 30 people remained. This is the first difficulty for the team. The team leader also went to major pharmacies to solicit donations of medicines. The results were also very disappointing, and there was a tendency to prevent the progress. Mr. Zhang could not think of a way, so he decided to sacrifice a finger to encourage morale, but he still secretly did not let people know his plan.

Oath Ceremony Yesterday, Mr. Zhang announced that the oath ceremony would be held in the afternoon. All team members arrived on time (only the remaining 30 people). The oath was taken in the large exercise field. As soon as the team members finished reading the oath, Captain Zhang took a sharp blade and cut off his middle finger, writing an oath in blood. Everyone was shocked, but Captain Zhang did not care, and said to everyone, "If I retreat in the middle of the way due to fear of difficulties, I will have such a finger." The team members were greatly moved, and some of the classmates who had not joined also joined as a result. The number of team members increased from 30 to 80. After completing the oath, Captain Zhang held his severed finger and went to major pharmacies to solicit donations of medicines. The results were very satisfactory. It is heard that he will set off soon, taking the Jinpu and Pingsui lines, and then walking to Heilongjiang from Zhangjiakou.

General Ma's Song 103

— Qian Xiaoshan

General Ma, a true general. His loyalty and righteousness reach the wind and clouds. The Japanese bandits are rampant and invading us urgently. Shenyang and Jilin were lost one after another early in the morning. Who will strengthen the border defense to support the army? Then teach thousands of miles without a strong wall. Is the corner of Longjiang not in danger? With you, it stands like a Great Wall. Holding a knife, he vowed to fight alone. It is good to collect my bones in horse skin. The righteous spirit has always moved gods and ghosts. Military reports were repeatedly reported three times a month. Alas, the affairs of the country are almost heartbreaking. Dare to say to defend against insults by strangling their throats. There are also those who hold soldiers and watch, and use their tongues to strike the thieves with loud voices. The battle at Jiangqiao was fierce, with dark clouds over the battlefield. No foreign aid was heard coming from the north. Do not expect to recover Beijing like Li Guo. You yourself are worthy of Zhang Suiyang. The little boy is deeply angry and has no inch of iron. A short song is attached to the chest. I wish you would complete this meritorious service of sweat and blood. Cast the bravery with hundred-refined gold. (This poem was just drafted, and the black wall has fallen. Those who sit and watch without saving are guilty to the sky.)

Storytelling Rotary Club

The Countryman Comes to Shanghai Again (Twenty-Four) 104

— Bao Tianxiao

Therefore, this time he came to Shanghai, he could be said to have gained an experience from the last time, learned a lesson, and saw that the sign was written on a certain hotel, he knew that this was not a real hotel, but a place for rich people to sleep. He saw many dressed-up and enchanting women coming in and out of that kind of hotel, and he remembered a common saying. The common saying says, "Opened a restaurant and not afraid of big bellies." This was originally said to mean that no matter how much food a person comes in, the restaurant can cope with it. Now, what kind of hotels in Shanghai, what kind of hotels, specialize in sleeping with women, which also corresponds to the saying - opened a restaurant and not afraid of big bellies - meaning: It doesn't matter if you make a big sister's belly bigger.

He knew that there was a hotel alley in Shanghai, and the hotels in that place were really places to eat, but he didn't know where the hotel alley was? Someone said, "The hotel alley has been demolished, and in the future, several floors of some kind of hotel will be built, and the real hotel will become a fake hotel." He turned a corner and saw many shops that seemed to be able to fill his belly. But he was a little timid and didn't dare to go in. At that time, he had to ask. Seeing a gentleman with a beard, he stepped forward to greet him and asked:

"Excuse me! Old sir! May I ask you a question! Is there a place to eat here?" The person he asked happened to be from Jiading, and he felt a little unhappy when he heard the words "old sir" in his heart. He wanted to make a few comments, but when he saw that it was an old countryman, he knew that he was unintentional, so he held back. He glanced at him and said:

"There are many places to eat. Aren't those on the left and right sides all restaurants?" The old gentleman from Jiading pointed to the left and right and hurried away.

The countryman looked in the direction he pointed, but the two red characters of the electric lights on the left were written "Taoyuan"; the two red characters of the electric lights on the right were written "Meiyuan".

He thought: Not good! I'm afraid I'm going to be fooled again. Taoyuan and Meiyuan are obviously the names of gardens. How can you say they are places to eat? I remember that in a small teahouse in our town, a storyteller who told the Romance of the Three Kingdoms came in the spring, and he said that Liu Guanzhang made a covenant in Taoyuan, didn't he have a Taoyuan? I didn't expect there to be a Taoyuan here, and I'm afraid Liu Guanzhang is still enshrined inside. As for Meiyuan, I heard that there is also a Meiyuan in Wuxi, and many people go to play when the plum blossoms are in bloom. This is obviously also a garden. Could it be that when it comes to Shanghai, it has become a restaurant? Running into the garden to eat, wouldn't it become a joke again?

He hesitated for a long time, but his stomach was rumbling with hunger, so he had to walk into Meiyuan. As soon as he walked in, he shouted, "Oh dear! It really is a garden! And it's a zoo!"

Extreme Chaos in the Securities and Bond Market 109

Eight types of bonds were suspended from trading in the morning due to sharp declines.

Market sentiment improved in the afternoon, and prices rebounded across the board.

Yesterday's market conditions for various bonds on the Chinese Merchant Securities Exchange were as follows: The National League's strong attitude toward the Japanese was ineffective, and the only way for China to save itself was through self-reliance. Market sentiment was increasingly chaotic. At the opening of the morning session, there was a very enthusiastic rush to sell by small investors, while investors were extremely reluctant to buy. Bond prices all fell sharply across the board, with the decline becoming more severe than the previous day. Eight types of bond futures were suspended from trading due to declines of 4 yuan, including the 1929 December Customs Bonds, the 1930 November Charity Bonds, the 2031 Next Month Bonds, the 2029 November Customs Bonds, and the November Consolidated Tax Bonds. The 1929 November Customs Bonds and the 1929 December Customs Bonds also experienced sharp declines and were suspended from trading in the second session. The situation in the market was extremely tense for a time, and small investors were particularly panicked. In the afternoon session, trading could not begin on time because margin calls had not been met. Market sentiment seemed to improve slightly due to slightly better news about the situation, and there was some trading in the gray market, with prices rebounding by about 1 yuan. Trading resumed after 4 p.m., and the market situation changed dramatically. Various parties aggressively bought in to cover their positions at low prices, demand was strong, and prices rose rapidly. Therefore, except for the bonds that had been suspended from trading in the morning, all others rose by 2-3 yuan compared to the morning, except for those with no trading in the afternoon. As a result, compared to the previous day, the 2029 December Customs Bonds rebounded by 0.3 yuan. The Reorganization Six percent Bonds, the Salary Reduction Salt Tax Bonds, and the Troops Reduction Principal Consolidated Tax Bonds only fell by about 1-2 yuan in the afternoon. The volatility of the bond market was unprecedented. Although market sentiment has stabilized somewhat due to the rebound in the bond market yesterday afternoon, it is feared that the situation is still not optimistic given the current environment. The total spot trading volume for the day was only 9,000 yuan, with futures trading reaching 9.9 million in the morning and only 3 million in the afternoon, for a total of 12.7 million yuan.

Foreign Rice Transactions Are Dull 117

Wenzhou Rice Continues to Arrive and Sell

Yesterday, the foreign rice market saw futures traders not selling, but neither domestic nor Changjiang groups inquired. The local market appetite was also weak. The overall market transactions were light, with only 100 tons of small twists for January opening at a price of 4 taels, 7 qian, and 2 fen. This cargo was originally sold by Xiangmao for 4 taels, 7 qian, and 5 fen, and has now fallen by another 3 fen. Only local markets are slightly managing spot goods, but the number of arrivals has been limited recently. Except for the continuous distribution of previously arrived goods, cargo owners are mainly holding firm, so the market has not seen a very drastic drop. However, for the market price to turn around, it is necessary for local merchants to sell smoothly. The total daily transaction volume was 600 bags of small twists, priced at 10 yuan, 0 jiao, 2 fen, and 2 li. In addition, 1,500 bags of newly arrived Wenzhou rice opened at a price of 10 yuan, 0 jiao, 2 fen, 9 li to 10 yuan, 0 jiao, 1 fen, 9 li, which was also managed by local markets.

Noodle Flour Market Listless 118

Distant Months Show More Stable Short Covering

Yesterday, the flour market saw similar opening prices in the morning and afternoon, with various months generally showing a flat trend. Tianjin wheat prices plummeted by 1.34 yuan, which were due to the unstable situation and the unusually tight money supply. Most people's minds have been shrinking. Due to the thick stocks of factories, preparations for the current month have not increased, gradually forming a hedging situation. Although distant months are also trending weakly, speculative shorts have gradually covered their positions, and the market atmosphere has been slightly more stable. Looking at future steps, if the money supply does not ease, the market will still not be good. As a result, the current month fell by 1.5 fen compared to the previous day, December fell by 1 fen and 2.5 li, January and February fell by 7.5 li, March fell by 1 fen, and April fell by 7.5 li.

Wheat Futures Plunge 6-7 Fen 119

Large-Scale Offloading by General Bulls

Yesterday, the wheat futures market opened in the morning and afternoon, with the market for each month showing a consistent plunge. Foreign ports suddenly reported a price decline of about 1.34 yuan, causing most people to feel unusually weak. Furthermore, given the domestic situation and the increasingly prepared appearance of Japan, if the trend becomes serious, the domestic prices of various markets are bound to become chaotic. Since the trend is not good, most bulls have also closed their positions, causing declines in both near and distant terms. The lowest price for the current month reached 3 taels, 5 qian, and 4 fen, seemingly close to the closing price of the previous month. As a result, the current month fell by 7 fen compared to the previous day, December fell by 6 fen, January and February fell by 5 fen, March fell by 4 fen, and April fell by 5 fen.

Southern and Northern Goods: Long-Term Shortage of Xiamen Tangerine Cakes Now Available 120

Previously, due to a shortage of Xiamen tangerine cake, the market price had risen to 21-22 taels, and then it was completely out of stock for a long time. Yesterday, it was heard that the Taikoo Company's Guangdong liner had arrived from Xiamen in the afternoon, bringing in a batch of Xiamen Tangerine Cakes; the exact number is unknown. This batch is likely to be new goods. Today is Sunday, so it will be necessary to take samples and open the market tomorrow.

Raw Silk, Tea, and Coarse Silk See Slight Increase in British Sales 121

Factory-Direct Prices See Small Increases - Hard to Judge the Trend

Yesterday, the raw silk market in Shanghai was still stagnant. Although there were telegrams from overseas white silk factories transferring to Shanghai, prices from American firms were only 850-860 taels, and prices from French firms were 870-880 taels. Factory owners are firmly maintaining prices. However, British firms have continued to make purchases of Coarse Silk, with firms such as Gong An purchasing 40 packages of Qian Da Silk, and prices remaining firm.

Sichuan-Hankou Silk Waste: European Sales Still Quiet 122

Silk Filature Purchases are Also Weak... Prices for Wild Silk Remain Depressed

Due to economic panic in Europe and the United States, sales of silk fabrics have been sluggish. Waste silk from filatures in Shanghai is also increasingly sporadic. With European sales not picking up, the market atmosphere is increasingly weak. Sales of wild silk to France are still quiet. Although Bailigu and Guyi had negotiations for Jingxian tails, Xiangcheng handles, and Hankou scarves yesterday, the offered prices were not high, and transactions are pending. Local silk filatures have also been making weak purchases of white silk waste. Yesterday, they only purchased 100 piculs of Inlands clothing silk, with prices ranging from 70 to 82 taels.

Tunxi Zhenmei Tea Transactions Are Strong 123

Shanghai Stocks Approximately 13,000 Boxes

Yesterday, the Tunxi Gaozhuang Zhenmei Green Tea market continued to see strong transactions. British firms such as Xiehe, Yihuo, Jinlong, and Tongfu have not loosened their buying intentions. There were also sporadic transactions of Needle Tip and Pearl Tea, and the market was not quiet. The total transaction volume for the city was over 800 boxes, with prices remaining unchanged from the past few days. According to statistics, current stock levels in the market are only about 13,000 boxes, which, according to general tea merchants, should be easily cleared within the year.

Inventory Survey of Hardware and Tinplate 124

The hardware market has also shown signs of gradually tightening during the recent tense national situation and financial market contraction. Although traders with ample cash flow had previously shown a tendency to expand, they have had to reduce their scope in the face of the recent perilous environment. As a result, the hardware market has seen little in the way of bulk transactions recently, except for sporadic transactions between door-to-door traders and factories. According to recent investigations, the most severely affected product in terms of market changes is tinplate. Pessimism is due to the belief among traders with inventory that the large amount of goods and slow sales will lead to unimaginable scenarios. As a result, the market is becoming increasingly weak, even to the point of collapsing, with losses reaching 5-6 taels per box. This is said to be the most drastic price decline since after the war. Therefore, traders in the market have deep concerns. However, to stabilize public sentiment, an inventory survey is being conducted to serve as a benchmark for market stabilization (unit: box).

Wang Jingwei Temporarily Stays in Shanghai 125

Will Not Return to Guangdong or Go to Beijing

Yesterday, the Guangdong Fourth Plenary Session Was Informed by Telegram

The Guangdong side dispatched Ma Chaojun and Tan Zhen to Shanghai to welcome Hu Hanmin and Wang Jingwei back to Guangdong to attend the Fourth Plenary Session of the Guangdong Provincial Committee. At the same time, the Beijing side also invited Hu and Wang to go to Beijing to preside over the major affairs of the party and the country. Yesterday, according to Wang Jingwei's aides, at a time when diplomacy is pressing and the national situation is critical, Wang has decided not to leave Shanghai temporarily and has informed the Fourth Plenary Session of the Guangdong Provincial Committee by telegram. It is absolutely untrue that the Beijing side has stated that Wang has agreed to go to Beijing immediately. It is said that Hu Hanmin also holds the same view. The telegram from the Fourth Plenary Session of the Guangdong Provincial Committee to Hu and Wang, and Wang's reply, are recorded below:

Mr. Hu Zhantang, Mr. Wang Jingwei:

In view of the national crisis, the major affairs of the party and the country await discussion. The extraordinary meeting and representatives have repeatedly telegraphed, urging the two gentlemen to come to Guangdong together on a fixed date, which is understandable. Today, the General Assembly unanimously resolved to invite the two gentlemen to return to Guangdong on a fixed date to attend and guide the meeting, and resolved to continue the formal meeting only after the two gentlemen return to Guangdong, in order to comply with the sincere request of colleagues. Please make an early trip and do not neglect to pray, the Fourth National Congress of the Chinese Kuomintang, issued from Guangzhou.

Wang Jingwei replied by telegram yesterday, reading:

The Fourth National Congress of the Chinese Kuomintang, Guangzhou:

I respectfully received your telegram. It is appropriate to attend the meeting, but the peace talks are mutually promoted by three comrades, Sun Zhesheng, Li Junpei, and Chen Youren, to return to Guangzhou to report. Zhaoming, Wu Tiyun, and Zou Haibin are in Shanghai to discuss various matters. This is the duty, and I dare not leave without permission. Recently, foreign aggression has become increasingly urgent and the national crisis is critical. I respectfully ask the General Assembly to convene a formal meeting as soon as possible, carry out all matters, establish the center of gravity of the party and the country, establish a guarantee of unity, and wish nothing but prayer. I hereby reply respectfully, I respectfully ask for your review. Wang Zhaoming, Ma.

In addition, it is reported that the Guangdong representatives in Shanghai, Wang Qingwei, Wu Chaochu, Zou Lu, etc., held two meetings with Ma Chaojun, Tan Zhen, etc. yesterday to discuss political and diplomatic issues. Regarding the election matters of the Fourth Plenary Session, it is heard that the Guangdong side, due to the urgency of time, must begin the election as early as the 24th of this month. Wang and others, after the meeting, immediately asked the Beijing representatives to request the Beijing Fourth Plenary Session to postpone its closing until after the 24th, so that both parties could complete the elections simultaneously.

All Sectors Urge the Government to Recover Lost Territories 126

A Glimpse of High Public Morale

The Anti-Japanese Association Submits a Document to the National Government Yesterday

Immediately Order the Army, Navy, and Air Force

To Recover the Lost Territories of the Northeast

The Shanghai Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association telegraphed the National Government yesterday, stating, "Presenting this as a request: Our Association's Committee Member Xie Fusheng's proposal states: Regarding the case of Japan's invasion and occupation of our Northeast territories, the League of Nations has given Japan until November 16th to withdraw its troops. Not only has Japan shown no intention of withdrawing, but it has also advanced to attack our Heilongjiang Province and disrupt Tianjin. In order to prevent the expansion of this incident, we must apply pressure to Japan and, in accordance with Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant, demand that member states of the League of Nations unanimously sever economic ties with Japan. Our government should first make a firm statement; otherwise, Japan will have nothing to fear, and the League of Nations will disregard us. Considering the diplomatic steps taken by the government, not only will this not hinder them, but it can also consolidate their foundation and expand their path. We request that the government resolutely implement this to maintain the nation's safety. Therefore, the proposed measures are listed below: (1) In accordance with Article 16 of the League of Nations Covenant, demand that member states of the League of Nations unanimously sever economic ties with Japan. (2) Our country's representative to the League of Nations should immediately propose measures under Article 16 and urge the League of Nations to further address the Northeast incident. (3) The government should invite Chinese and foreign journalists to formally announce and formulate laws to punish people who buy and sell Japanese goods, so that the boycott of Japanese goods can have a legal basis and assistance. The above proposal was approved by the 14th Executive Committee meeting of our Association, and it was requested that the National Government immediately use force to recover the lost territories of the Northeast and record it. Based on the above circumstances, we hereby submit this document for your kind review and approval for implementation, and request that you immediately order the Army, Navy, and Air Force to use force to recover the lost territories of the Northeast and restore our country's territory, which would be for the public good. Respectfully submitted to the National Government."

Telegram 1: To the Fourth National Congress in Nanjing: The Japanese are invading us, and the entire nation is filled with shared animosity. However, millions of soldiers advocate non-resistance and shamelessly cling to life, losing territory and disgracing the country, which is heartbreaking to speak of.
