However, due to exhausted ammunition and no reinforcements, the army was defeated, and the province was lost. The entire nation grieves. Therefore, the representatives dare to make a request to all of you, hoping you will carefully consider it. Zhang Xueliang, holding 300,000 troops, knows that the Heilongjiang army's resistance against Japan is a disparity in numbers, and the army is isolated and weak. A long battle is sure to fail. Yet, he ultimately does not mobilize a single soldier or general, treating the survival of Heilongjiang Province as if he does not see it. What are his intentions? It is truly suspicious. They are soldiers who are supposed to defend the territory but instead sell it, indulging in their duties, and nothing is worse than this. Is Heilongjiang Province not our land, and are the people of Heilongjiang not our army? If they are not senseless and insane, how could they go this far? Considering this comprehensively, even if they do not intend to collude with the Japanese in practice, they are bound to be close to betraying the country. (Omission) Therefore, the representatives, with tears of blood, bow again and again, pleading for the people of Heilongjiang, and for the survival of the nation, dare to request that Zhang Xueliang be ordered to proceed to Heilongjiang with the entire army by a specific date to assist Ma Zhanshan and recover the three provinces, and that Commander Chiang be ordered to dispatch troops to the border to strengthen national defense and fulfill his duties. Fourth Army Commander Zhang Fakui has already requested permission to depart to promote the national cause, and the government authorities should understand his patriotic fervor and provide him with the necessary facilities so that he can serve on the battlefield and fulfill his long-cherished wish. The telegram is filled with sorrow and urgency. We humbly request your consideration. Respectfully, the Student Delegation of Guangdong Province, Guangxi Province, and Guangzhou City."

Telegram 2: To National Revolutionary Fourth Army Commander Zhang, Upon Reading Your Telegram: Your patriotic fervor overflows your words, and your righteous indignation stirs the divine land. You vow to die with the soldiers who serve the country and do not wish to exist with the soldiers who shamelessly do not resist. This heart and this ambition are worthy of song and tears. Your loyalty is deeply admired. The representatives are willing to use their blood and sincerity, together with the students of Guangdong and Guangxi provinces, to be your backing, earnestly requesting that you immediately dispatch troops to assist Heilongjiang, annihilate the Japanese invaders, and return our territory. The telegram expresses our heartfelt wishes. Respectfully, the Student Delegation of Guangdong Province, Guangxi Province, and Guangzhou City Attending the National Student Anti-Japanese Congress."

Zhang Fakui Speaks of His Determination to Assist Heilongjiang 128

Willing to Die in the Same Place as Chairman Ma

Zhang Fakui, Commander of the National Revolutionary Fourth Army, has been in Shanghai for several days seeking medical treatment. Previously, due to his abhorrence of Japanese atrocities and Ma Zhanshan's isolated army resisting Japan without assistance, he telegraphed Guangdong requesting permission to volunteer. It is now heard that Guangdong has expressed great support for Zhang's request, but there has been no official reply. A reporter from the Xinsheng News Agency paid him a visit yesterday and spoke with him. At the same time, the reporter, representing the Northeast Hometown Anti-Japanese Association, had some contact regarding the practical work of assisting Heilongjiang. Here is a record of his conversation in the capacity of receiving representatives: (1) Guangdong has not yet replied to the request to volunteer, but it is expected that there will be a reply soon, and it can be confidently asserted that the request will be approved. The reason why a reply could not be given immediately is that Guangdong is currently holding the Fourth Plenary Session, and this matter must be resolved through deliberation. It is expected that in the future, Commanders Li and Bai will also have important statements. (2) Assisting Heilongjiang requires the troops to be transferred to Heilongjiang Province and merged with Ma's forces. Although the troops under my command are not numerous, we all believe that the amount of troops is not important. Even I personally can serve as a low-ranking officer to provide assistance. I have this determination, not because I want to show off. When assisting in the future, it would be even better if we can achieve contact with Ma's army. Otherwise, I personally am willing to die in the same place as Chairman Ma. (3) The current government does not seek self-reliance but relies on the League of Nations, which is quite strange. China has millions of troops nationwide. If it is said that they cannot compete with Japan, I find it hard to believe. Although Japanese weapons are extremely well-equipped, if everyone in China has the determination to sacrifice, using one hundred to fight against one, it would be enough to kill the Japanese. If the government says that sending troops is a war against Japan, then that is even more incorrect. Sending troops is to assist the anti-Japanese forces, and anti-Japanese action is out of self-defense, which is different from Japan's dispatch of troops to invade and occupy the three Northeastern Provinces. Since Japan is already engaging in acts of war against us, why can't our country even defend itself? Ma Zhanshan is only a brigade commander, yet he is able to resist such a heavy force, which is truly admirable. The Japanese troops attacking Heilongjiang are increasing daily, but our government has not sent a single soldier or general to provide assistance, sitting idly by while this isolated army is trapped in a desperate situation, which is regrettable. (4) Zhang Xueliang lost the land of Liaoning and Jilin this time and did not send troops to assist Ma Zhanshan. From a military perspective, he should have apologized to the people long ago. Why should he wait for the government and the people to discuss it? (5) The people's hearts in the country are not dead, and public morale is exceptionally indignant. In the future, when it becomes unbearable, the people will inevitably rise up on their own to resist the violent Japanese.

The Shanghai New Medicine Trade Association sent a letter to Zhang Fakui yesterday, stating, "To Commander Zhang, Upon reading your telegram, we were deeply moved to tears. Since the founding of the Republic of China, only General Han and Chairman Ma have pointed their guns outward. Your Excellency resolutely steps forward to eliminate demons and monsters for the world and to fight for the survival of the Chinese nation. Your loyal heart and fierce courage move people and heaven. Our Association is willing to respectfully offer provisions and comfort the righteous army. However, it is heard that the dispatch of the elite troops is still awaiting the issuance of a government order. Although this is a discipline that soldiers should abide by, in special circumstances, as long as one's conscience is clear, it seems permissible to act according to circumstances. The return of Yue Fei's army was a source of regret for the people. We hope Your Excellency will consider this deeply."

The Case of the Japanese Consulate General Illegally Arresting Returning Overseas Chinese 134

One of the Detained Overseas Chinese is Named Zhang Debao

The Japanese Consulate General Claims that Zhang Committed a Crime in Japan

Without Prior Permission from Our Country's Authorities

Section Chief Huang of the Public Security Bureau Negotiated Yesterday

The Huadong News Agency reports: The Japanese Consulate General in this port illegally arrested one of our country's overseas Chinese on the Japanese ship Nagasaki Maru, which came to Shanghai from Japan, at 2:00 PM the day before yesterday. At around 6:00 PM on the same day, when the Japanese ship Rokko Maru entered the port, the Consulate General again sent personnel to arrest returning overseas Chinese. At that time, it was rumored that as many as four people had been illegally arrested by the Consulate General. At this time of strained relations between China and Japan, all sectors of Shanghai were extremely indignant upon hearing this. After receiving this report, the Municipal Public Security Bureau immediately sent personnel to investigate the truth. It was found that when the Nagasaki Maru entered the port, the Japanese Consulate General did illegally arrest our returning overseas Chinese citizen. The detained overseas Chinese is named Zhang Debao, who recently returned from Tochigi Prefecture, Japan. As for the Japanese ship Rokko Maru at 6:00 PM on the afternoon of the question, although the Japanese Consulate General sent personnel to search, no one was detained. After receiving the report, the Municipal Public Security Bureau believed that the Consulate General had not notified our country's authorities beforehand and had arbitrarily arrested returning overseas Chinese, which was extremely illegal. The Director of the Public Security Bureau, Chen Xizeng, sent the Second Section Chief of the Bureau, Huang Guangdou, to the Japanese Consulate General yesterday to negotiate and thoroughly investigate the truth. The Japanese Consulate General replied verbally that the arrested overseas Chinese Zhang Debao, on the evening of the 11th of this month, in Kurosu Town, Tochigi Prefecture, Japan, together with overseas Chinese Jin He Biao, committed the crime of plotting to kill the Chinese merchant Lin Shunan, who had been living in Japan for a long time, for money. Afterwards, they carried the money and fled back to China. The police station in that county telegraphed the Japanese Consulate General in Shanghai, requesting that Zhang and others be arrested when they came to Shanghai in order to extradite them back to Japan. When the Nagasaki Maru entered the port, only Zhang Debao was arrested. Therefore, at around 6:00 PM, they searched the entering Rokko Maru again. As a result, Jin He Biao was not found. Therefore, only Zhang Debao was arrested the day before yesterday. After listening, Section Chief Huang negotiated, asking why the authorities of our country were not notified in advance, and returned to overseas Chinese without authorization. Regardless of whether the cases committed are true or not, the procedures are not in compliance. He immediately negotiated verbally with the Japanese Consulate General, requesting extradition, and on the other hand, returned to the bureau to report to Director Chen. It is heard that the Japanese Consulate General has not yet made any statement regarding the extradition. The Public Security Bureau has already submitted the facts to the Municipal Government and requested serious negotiations.

Japanese Thugs Provoke Trouble in Zhabei, Japanese Consulate General Expresses Apologies 135

And Promises to Punish the Japanese Who Caused the Incident

Huadong News Agency reports: At around 1:00 PM the day before yesterday, four Japanese thugs suddenly appeared at the Zhabei branch of the Anti-Japanese Association inside the Zhongxing Theater on Zhongxing Road. Three were wearing Western suits and one was wearing Chinese clothes. They led more than forty Japanese thugs disguised in Chinese clothes, carrying wooden sticks and hiring three cargo trucks, hoping to forcibly transport the sealed scrap iron from the site. At that time, the situation was very serious, and the large number of Japanese thugs in Chinese clothes with weapons were especially aggressive in their provocations. The branch immediately telegraphed the Fifth District Police Station under its jurisdiction. After receiving the report, District Chief Wang Zhijing immediately sent staff member Zhou Chunyu, supervisor Ren Runsheng, and the police chief to suppress the incident. At that time, a large number of Japanese thugs fled upon hearing the news, while the four Japanese ringleaders were detained by the Anti-Japanese Association branch. District Chief Wang then took them to the Fifth Police Station for questioning. It was learned that the four ringleaders, the one wearing Chinese clothes was named Nakamura Nagayoshi, and the other three were named Nagawoku, Hosotani Nara, and Nakamura Kan, all residing at No. 60 Xingye Lane, Shigaota Road. They were instigated by a Japanese named Sai, which led to this unreasonable act. At that time, the Municipal Public Security Bureau also telegraphed the Japanese Consulate General, questioning the large number of Japanese thugs

The Japanese Consulate General sent Yoshitake Kazuo and Akaboshi Kazuki to the Fifth District Headquarters to request extradition. At that time, they deeply apologized for the excessive actions of these Japanese thugs and were willing to bring them back for punishment. The Fifth District Police Station agreed, and they were extradited back. Yesterday, the Municipal Public Security Bureau reported the situation to the Municipal Government.

At 2:00 PM on the 20th of this month, more than forty Japanese thugs, each holding wooden sticks and weapons, threatened to enter the storage department of the Zhabei Inspection Station of the Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association to forcibly loot the confiscated Japanese goods. At that time, the situation was quite tense, and nearby residents

were frightened. Zhou Xuechang Suppresses the People's Movement

Appealing to the Press for Justice

Ms. Sun Xiangjie, a representative of the Beiping Women's Anti-Japanese Association, the National Salvation Association, and the Middle School Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association, hosted the local press at the New Richard's Restaurant at 2:00 PM yesterday to report on the truth of Zhou Xuechang, the Organizing Committee Member of the Beiping Municipal Party Department and Director of the Municipal Education Bureau, suppressing the anti-Japanese movement, and appealed to the press to uphold justice. Sincerely, etc. We are sending this letter for your perusal and implementation.

The Chamber of Commerce Replies to the Paper Industry Association: The Municipal Chamber of Commerce yesterday addressed the matter of handling and sealing up Japanese goods in a letter to the Paper Industry Association, stating: "To whom it may concern, on the 20th of this month, we received a letter stating that the Cotton Industry Association and others were urging a resolution on the method of handling Japanese goods. When Luo Qinghua convened a dinner and presented the original letter, requesting the association's seal, he was not granted permission. Why is the Paper Industry Association still listed in the newspaper report? Please investigate and clarify." The following is a detailed response: (1) The letter from the Cotton Cloth Industry Association and eighteen other associations to our association urging a resolution on the method of handling Japanese goods does indeed list your association and bears your association's seal. The documents are all on file and can be inspected by your association's representatives. (2) According to a statement from Mr. Luo Qinghua, the dinner that day was convened by Mr. Ye Xiaoshan of the Cotton Cloth Industry Association in the name of Luo Qinghua et al. of the Shanghai Merchants Club Preparatory Office. During the dinner, someone mentioned whether the Silk and Satin Industry Association should affix its seal, and the response was that the matter of affixing the seal should be discussed with the association. Given that the Silk and Satin Industry Association did not affix its seal in this case, there was no reason to persuade other industries to affix their seals. This can be used as evidence to the contrary. We hereby reply to your association for your review and immediate publication of a correction to reflect the facts. Furthermore, this type of matter is of great importance to the reputation of organizations. The facts should be verified first and not hastily published. We hope that you will be cautious in the future. This is of utmost importance. To the Shanghai Paper Industry Association.

Their ambition is increasing without end. This kind of violent act violates the Nine-Power Treaty and destroys the Kellogg-Briand Pact. Although the League of Nations has repeatedly urged Japan to withdraw its troops, Japan has always ignored it. Now, it has intensified its actions, dared to attack Heilongjiang Province, and occupied Qiqihar on the Eastern Railway on a convenient day. Japan has violated Article 15, Paragraph 6 of the League of Nations Covenant. Therefore, the Board of Directors should immediately invoke Article 16 of the Covenant and implement more effective sanctions to ensure world peace and maintain the prestige of the League of Nations. If the League of Nations continues to procrastinate and fail to uphold justice and effectively urge Japan to withdraw its troops against this country that disregards international treaties, destroys peace in the Far East, and endangers world peace, China will have to seek its own defense to restore its territorial and administrative integrity and safeguard world justice and humanity. The current situation is serious and has reached its limit. The Chinese people unanimously oppose the five principles or compromises proposed by Japan in the League of Nations, and we absolutely cannot recognize the Twenty-One Demands that China was previously forced to sign under Japanese oppression. Moreover, direct negotiations are not allowed under this kind of military threat unless Japan fulfills its treaty obligations and withdraws its troops. China will not accept other mediation conditions. We hope that you will convey this message to the women's organizations of the countries that have signed the League of Nations Covenant, the Nine-Power Treaty, and the Kellogg-Briand Pact, and ask them to urge their respective governments to fulfill their obligations under the above three treaties and sanction Japan's atrocities with strength. Sincerely, Ding Shujing and Ma of the National Association of the Chinese Christian Women's Youth Association.

Municipal Chamber of Commerce Announces Prohibition of Raising Prices of National Goods 142

The Shanghai Municipal Chamber of Commerce issued an urgent notice yesterday regarding the prohibition of raising the prices of national goods. The notice stated that the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau Instruction No. 16769 was issued based on the Ministry of Industry Instruction No. Zi 8562. The Ministry of Industry stated that in February of this year, it received a report from the Fujian National Goods Promotion Association requesting a prohibition on raising the prices of national goods, and it had ordered the bureau to issue a notice. In June, the Executive Yuan issued a letter from the Central Secretariat based on a report from the Hubei Provincial Party Headquarters requesting a strict prohibition on unscrupulous merchants raising prices after , and a circular was issued to each agency. Now, it is reported that at a time when the national goods movement is being vigorously promoted, there are still merchants who transport and sell national goods who disregard the overall situation, seek petty profits, and take the opportunity to raise prices, which is extremely abhorrent. It is important to know that the higher the price of national goods, the smoother the sale of foreign goods. This not only infringes upon the interests of the owner, but also undermines the progress of the nation. It is appropriate to reiterate the previous order and order the chamber of commerce to convene industrialists and merchants to form a national goods evaluation committee to investigate the national goods sold on the market in detail and immediately reduce the prices of those who have raised prices. At the same time, the public should be notified that if unscrupulous merchants raise prices, they will be allowed to report them by name and be punished accordingly to serve as a warning and to encourage others. In response to this, the 20th Executive Committee of the Chamber decided that the selection of members for the evaluation committee should be submitted to the Standing Committee. All matters relating to the prohibition of raising the prices of national goods will be announced to the industrial and commercial sectors of the city for compliance. It is hereby announced in the newspaper that all national goods industrial and commercial sectors are expected to comply.

The Municipal Government Allocates Funds for Dredging the Suzhou River 143

Mayor Zhang of the Municipal Government previously determined to dredge the Suzhou River due to its siltation, which hindered water traffic. He decided to dredge the section from Waibaidu Bridge to Yuji Mound, which is the most important. It has already been opened to the bottom of Xizang Road. The funds for dredging the river have also been discussed and agreed upon, with the Municipal Government allocating 20,000 taels per year. More Local News on the Following Page 145

Page 19

Local News Two

Kidnapping Bandits Kidnap the Wrong God of Wealth 146

The City Bank President is Safe and Sound

The Accountant of Huiwentang Acts as a Representative

The Bandits Seize the Yuejie Police Officer's Gun Mid-Kidnapping

Fortunately, Xu Fu's Two Sons Temporarily Changed Their Surnames

At around 10 o'clock yesterday morning, a kidnapping case occurred at the corner of Avenue Joffre and Rue Bédier in the French Concession, where the bandits mistakenly kidnapped the wrong person. The real target of the kidnapping was Xu Fu, a well-known former Chief of the Accounting Office of the National Revolutionary Army General Headquarters, Director of the Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau, and current President of the Shanghai City Bank. However, the bandits confusedly kidnapped Lin Yongming, the accountant of the Huiwentang Printing Bureau at No. 5 Henan Road. This substitution is rare in kidnapping cases. When our reporter visited last night, President Xu and his relatives were gathered together, enjoying themselves. The details of the incident are as follows:

Xu Fu Has Held Important Positions: Xu Fu, courtesy name Shengchan, is in his fifties and is a native of Zhenhai, Zhejiang. He once served as Chief of the Accounting Office of the National Revolutionary Army General Headquarters and Director of the Shanghai Municipal Finance Bureau, among other important positions. He is currently the President of the Shanghai City Bank (on Tianjin Road) and resides in a large building at No. 15 Deqing Lane, Tongfu Lane, Avenue Joffre, French Concession. Xu has two sons, the elder named Zhengjiao, 19 years old, a student at Fudan University, and the younger named Zhengxing, 14 years old, who is being tutored at home. Xu is well aware that he has held prominent positions. In view of the rampant kidnapping in Shanghai, he specially purchased two cars as a precaution to avoid the attention of bandits.

Yesterday in a Small Roadster: Xu's two cars are a new Buick sedan, Concession No. 10199 (City No. 5392), and an old-fashioned light gray Austin roadster, Concession No. 7256 (City No. 1366). Xu usually takes the sedan when attending formal banquets. When going to the bank for office work, Xu usually takes the roadster. Yesterday happened to be the first month anniversary of Xu's eldest grandson, and many relatives and friends came to congratulate him. At around 9:00 yesterday morning, Xu took the roadster to the bank for office work, while the sedan remained at home to welcome guests.

Four Bandits Block the Car: At 10:15 AM, Xu's two sons, along with Lin Yongming (38 years old, Xu's fellow villager), an accountant at the Huiwentang Printing Bureau at No. 5 Henan Road, Xu Xingwu (40 years old), an accountant at Xu's residence, and a servant of Xu, along with the driver Zhu Shunyuan (36 years old, from Funing), a total of six people, went out in the sedan. As the car was leaving the alley to the east and approaching Chen Ruiyu's Shunyuan Cigarette and Paper Shop at No. 14 Rue Bédier corner, bandits suddenly emerged from a four-way intersection. One bandit with a gun first approached the servant, suspecting that he was the bodyguard. Another bandit threatened the driver.

Yuejie Police Officer's Gun is Seized: The driver and servant were dragged out of the car by the bandits. At that time, Yuejie Police Officer No. 262 was patrolling by and was about to draw his gun to help, but two bandits had already surrounded him, monitored him, and seized the gun he was wearing. Then, they all boarded the car, and one bandit drove north like a flight. The driver saw the car being seized and frantically shouted after it, watching as the car went east on Avenue Foch and then straight onto Avenue Edward VII. At that time, a business car happened to pass by, and the driver stopped it, explained the situation, and quickly got into the car and chased east at full speed. However, when he chased near the Great World, the No. 10199 car had disappeared.

Xu Fu's Two Sons Change Their Surnames: The driver had no choice but to rush back to tell the owner and report it to the French Police Station. The police chief used the telephone to notify all the police stations in the Public Concession and the districts and departments of the Public Security Bureau to pay attention to interception. Meanwhile, the car was handed over to the private detectives to be taken to a special agency for questioning. However, in less than an hour, while the police were interrogating the driver, Xu's two sons and the accountant Xu Xingwu were sent to the French Police Station by the Yangshupu Police Station. According to the accountant, the bandits questioned them in the car, first asking who Xu's two relatives were. The accountant said that one's surname was Zhang and the other's surname was Li, and they were going to Xu's residence to offer congratulations. The bandits did not suspect anything, but only paid attention to Lin Yongming.

Xu Fu's Business Card is Found: One bandit immediately searched Lin's body and found a business card of Xu Fu. He was overjoyed, thinking that he must be the president. When the car arrived near Dalian Bay Road, he drove out the rest of us and took Lin alone. The three of us rushed to report to the Yangshupu Police Station, thus escaping danger, etc. At around 12:00 noon, the French Police Station received a phone call from the Yangshupu Police Station saying that the No. 10199 car had been found in the middle of Lan Road. The French Police detectives and the driver Zhu Shunyuan took the car and rushed to the scene. It was indeed the car that had been seized, so they drove it back to Xu's residence.

The Accountant Has News of Leaving Danger: When our reporter heard the news, he went to Xu's residence to inquire. He only saw large and small cars parked at the entrance of the alley. The sound of firecrackers could be heard from inside the house. After the reporter submitted his card, the family member lowered his voice and said respectfully, "The president is busy and unable to see guests. The kidnapped person has nothing to do with the president, so there is no need to extend an interview." At this point, the reporter understood. He then went to Huiwentang to inquire. According to the staff of the bureau, Lin only has an income of 40 yuan per month. In his hometown, there are three sons, three daughters, a wife, and a mother who depend on him for their livelihood. He is not qualified to be kidnapped. He must have been taken by mistake. Finally, he said that he had heard that Lin had left danger, but where he is now and whether it is true remains to be proven.

Follow-up Report on the Hanyang Steamer Robbery 150

No Major Losses

The Robbers Did Not Abduct Anyone

The Taikoo Company's Hanyang steamer, which sailed from Shanghai to Nanhua, had 15 pirates mixed in. It was reported yesterday that they suddenly robbed the ship at sea near Nan'ao, near Xiamen. It is now known that after the ship was robbed, it was slightly tidied up and then sailed to Xiamen. Yesterday morning, the company received a telegram from Hanyang stating that the ship had arrived in Xiamen and was unloading cargo and will depart for Hong Kong today.

Robbed Goods: This time, the pirates aimed to rob a large sum of cash. They were very disappointed when they realized they had boarded the wrong ship. They robbed passengers and cargo. It was found that the cargo loaded in Shanghai this time included 620 pieces of cotton yarn and foreign cloth, 710 pieces of native cloth, 600 pieces of cotton, and leather goods and cigarettes. After investigation, it was found that the robbed items were cotton yarn, piece goods, and part of the leather goods. The exact amount is not yet known and will be clear after the entire ship has been unloaded.

Telegraph Inquiry About Lost Goods: Yesterday, the company sent a telegram to Hanyang asking them to investigate the number of pieces and marks of the lost goods in order to notify the customers. As for the passengers who were robbed, it was reported that there were no major losses. Only the money and jewelry they were carrying were robbed. The crew and passengers were not kidnapped.

British Warship Pursues: After this incident, the British warship stationed in Hong Kong has dispatched a ship to pursue the pirates towards Dapeng Bay.

Continued Transport of Large Sums of Money: 6 million yuan in cash was transported from this port to Dalian. The shipment on board aroused the pirates' covetousness, resulting in the mistaken robbery of the Hanyang steamer. Yesterday, another large sum of 1,105,000 yuan in cash was loaded to Dalian. Originally, it was intended to load 1.4 million yuan, but because the purchase in Shanghai was incomplete, 221 boxes were loaded first, including 50 boxes loaded by two banks, totaling 250,000 yuan. The rest were transported by Nanrongji and are scheduled to be exported today.

Using a Bullet as a Gift 152

Xiao Yinghua Forces Acceptance

Extortion Investigation: Handwriting Comparison

Hong Meiji, the owner of the Chunhe Yong woolen and foreign goods store at number 83 Dongqi Street, residing at number 22 Hongxing Lane, North Sichuan Road, received a threatening letter on the 16th of this month. The letter, bearing the name "Wuxia Group," was filled with extremely threatening language, intending to extort 10,000 yuan. It stated that if the money was to be delivered, a red paper should be posted at the store's entrance, and someone would come to negotiate. Hong ignored the letter. On the afternoon of the day before yesterday, at 3 p.m., a Cantonese man named Xiao Yinghua came to Chunhe Yong with a box of cigarettes and two bottles of wine, claiming they were a gift from a Mr. Zhang to Boss Hong. The store staff informed Hong, who refused to accept them, stating he had no friend or relative named Zhang. He secretly sent a staff member, Ge Jianyun, to follow Xiao. Ge saw Xiao leave the store and head north, turning into Sima Road at Henan Road, then turning again to Jiangxi Road before circling back to Chunhe Yong on Dongqi Pan Street. He insisted Zhang required the gifts to be accepted. Hong opened the cigarette box and found no cigarettes, only a letter. He opened the letter and found another threatening message, along with a bullet. Hong reported this to Detective Huang Fusen, who arrested Xiao and detained him in the General Police Station. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the First Special Court's Criminal Division. Police lawyer Li Zhishan explained the case, stating the police were prosecuting according to Article 1, Paragraph 2 of the Regulations for Punishing Bandits and Article 370 of the Criminal Code. However, the case still required further investigation, and an extension was requested. Ge Jianyun and others then testified. When questioned, the defendant claimed Zhu asked him to deliver the items, and he didn't know what they were. He denied writing the letters. Judge Xu Jiashi then ordered the defendant to write numbers in court for handwriting comparison. After Xiao wrote them, Judge Xu questioned him further and then ordered the defendant back into custody for further questioning at a later date.

Daughter's Lawsuit Against Father Self-Terminates 153

Plaintiff Claims Father-Daughter Relationship, Voluntarily Withdraws Lawsuit

The case of Song Xueqin, a prominent official, being sued by his former concubine, Bo Xuezhen, in the name of his daughter, Song Lizhen, has had the defendant, Song Xueqin's, written defense published in this newspaper. Yesterday morning, the case resumed in the First Special District Court, presided over by Judge Guo Shouyi. The plaintiff's lawyer, Jiang Yiping, stated that the plaintiff's legal guardian, Bo Xuezhen, was still ill and unable to attend. The plaintiff requested permission to withdraw the case due to the father-daughter relationship. Judge Guo then asked the defendant's lawyer for his opinion. The defendant's lawyer, Wang Chuanbi, stated that since the plaintiff recognized their mistake, it was fine to drop the case. Thus, the case of the seven-year-old daughter suing her father ended.

Jing'an Temple Dispute Resolved 154

Zhi Fa, the abbot of Jing'an Temple, sued Zhi Wen, the former abbot who had been relieved of his duties, for gathering Chen Ze Wo, Yao Fuqing, Gu Tingfang, Sha Shouzhong, Feng Xie, Feng Guangjia, Wang Dezhang, Wang Yunzeng, and others, to disturb the temple and damage property. Zhi Wen and Chen Yao also sued for illegal detention and obstruction. The dispute between the two sides was fierce, with multiple court sessions and inquiries. Yesterday, Judge Xiao Xiefei mediated the dispute in court, advising Zhi Fa, as the abbot of a large temple, to be generous and tolerant, and that as a monk, he should be indifferent to worldly matters and endure everything. He suggested Yao Fuqing and others apologize orally to resolve the matter, considering their age. Zhi Fa initially refused, arguing that the matter was caused by the other party disturbing him and falsely accusing him, and that they should apologize. However, after Judge Xiao repeatedly persuaded him, and lawyers Wu Chengyu and Chen Ruixiang stated they respected the court's ruling, Zhi Fa stood up and respectfully apologized to the court. Chen Yao and others quickly left, thus ending the Jing'an Temple lawsuit that had stirred up society.

Large Group of Robbers Convicted 155

The bandit Ji Wenhua, from Sichuan, used a car with fake credentials to transport his accomplices Du Qi, Yu Hengdao, and others on the evening of the sixth of last month. They were armed and intended to rob a certain family's property in the Four Da Lane on Kangti Road in the French Concession. As the car stopped, before they could act, detectives Jin Jiulin, Li Yaolong, Qian Yumin, Mao Jingeng, Zhang Ziying, Bao Tan Qin Yu, and Zhou Buguang from the French Concession's special investigation unit arrived. Du and Yu noticed them and fled. The detectives arrested Ji along with the car. Later, they arrested Du and Yu, as well as six other individuals involved: Hu Naiguang (the car owner), Qian Guangshu, Yu Bulou, etc. They confiscated pistols, bullets, military banknotes, and other items. They discovered that the bandits had previously robbed three families: number 33 and number 38 Baoxing Lane, and the Chen Wang family on Saipo Road. Qian was also connected to the case where Wu Yanfang, the accountant of the Ruikang Paint Store, was kidnapped and jumped to his death. They were sent to the Second Special District Court. After repeated interrogations by Judge Ge Zhitan, the defendants confessed to the robbery. The court appointed lawyers Xu Yannian and Shan Yuhua to provide pro bono defense for the defendants. The court declared the trial concluded and awaited sentencing. Yesterday, the sentencing was carried out. At 2:30 PM, Judge Ge presided over the Criminal Division Two courtroom and ordered the defendants to be brought in. After questioning their ages and origins, he announced the sentences. Ji Wenhua was sentenced to three years imprisonment for conspiracy to commit robbery, four years imprisonment for two counts of aiding and abetting armed robbery, and four years imprisonment for one count of conspiracy to commit armed robbery with breaking and entering at night. The sentences are to run consecutively for a total of seven years. Du Qi was sentenced to seven years imprisonment for two counts of armed robbery, and four years imprisonment for one count of conspiracy to commit armed robbery with breaking and entering at night. The sentences are to run consecutively for a total of eight years. Yu Hengdao was sentenced to three years imprisonment for conspiracy to commit robbery, seven years imprisonment for two counts of armed robbery, and four years imprisonment for one count of conspiracy to commit armed robbery with breaking and entering at night. The sentences are to run consecutively for a total of nine years. Hu Naiguang was sentenced to three years and six months imprisonment for aiding and abetting conspiracy to commit armed robbery with breaking and entering at night, and three years and six months imprisonment for possession of military bullets with intent to commit a crime. The sentences are to run consecutively for a total of five years. Yu Bulou was sentenced to six months imprisonment for receiving stolen goods. Qian Guangshu was sentenced to twelve years imprisonment for aiding and abetting kidnapping for ransom, and four years imprisonment for aiding and abetting armed robbery. The sentences are to run consecutively for a total of thirteen years. The number of days of detention prior to the final judgment will be credited at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment. Four pistols, thirty-five bullets, one used four-cylinder yellow Chevrolet car, and two credentials were confiscated. Thirty-two yuan in Central Bank temporary exchange coupons, one Mark currency note, and one large and one small genuine credential from the car are to be sent to the court for safekeeping. After sentencing, the defendants were taken back into custody to await further instructions.

Page 20

After Qin was arrested and executed, Shen fled to Shanghai, keeping his whereabouts secret, making it difficult to apprehend him. To the team leader to take him back to Changzhou, return to the case for interrogation.

Various Groups Emphasize Housing Disputes in Yixin Lane 157

The housing dispute in the Yixin Lane area of Nanjing Road has now been brought to court, and a trial has been held once, with a postponement for retrial, as reported in previous newspapers. It is now known that since this case occurred, various groups in Shanghai have paid close attention to rental disputes. Because it is a time of internal and external troubles, the market is very depressed, but landlords and homeowners only care about their own interests, regardless of the suffering of others. Rent increases and forced evictions are common. This matter has a significant relationship with the housing rights of all citizens. If it is not corrected urgently, it is unimaginable what the disaster will be. More than 30 groups, including the Shanghai Citizens' Union First District Branch, plan to submit a large-scale petition to various agencies based on Shanghai's rental customs to avoid the suffering of all stores and residents in the city from having no houses to live in, and not to allow the total land ownership equalization for the benefit of the people to be destroyed by a few wealthy merchants.

Suddenly Seeing a Fellow Townsman Holding a Lost Daughter 158

Cutting Off Small Braids Suddenly Changes Appearance

Planning to Be Inducted Into a Brothel to Learn Prostitution

Gen Chang, the five-year-old daughter of Li Aliulu from Yancheng, residing at number 497 Gordon Road, disappeared at 1:30 PM on the 17th of this month while playing in front of the door. People were entrusted to search everywhere, but there was no news. Unexpectedly, at around 2:00 PM the day before yesterday, Li Aliulu was passing through Miller Road when he saw Guo Sanyuan, a fellow townsman, holding his daughter and entering the house at number 678 on that road. He immediately reported this to the Chinese constables at number 2897 to enter together and arrest Guo. Together with the girl Gen Chang, they were taken to the head of the Hongkou Police Station, who ordered them to be detained. The girl was handed over to her father, Li Aliulu, to be taken back. Yesterday morning, the police sent Guo to the Criminal Division Two of the First Special Court. According to police lawyer Zhang Tianyin, the girl Gen Chang pointed out that the defendant had cut off the small braid she had been keeping on her head, changed her hairstyle, and changed her clothes. This was to sell her to a brothel to learn prostitution. Furthermore, the defendant had previously run a brothel, please postpone the investigation to see if there are any other cases, etc. Subsequently, the plaintiff, Li Aliulu, explained the situation, but the girl Gen Chang did not answer a word when asked because of the crowd in the courtroom. When questioned, the defendant's confession was vague, claiming that the girl was abducted by someone else, begging for consideration. After Shen Bingrong corroborated the confession, he ordered him to be remanded back into custody for further investigation at a later date.

Printing Illegal Horseracing Lottery Tickets Sentenced 159

Li Liansheng, the chief detective of the anti-gambling squad of the French Concession Police, and Liu Kunbao, the deputy detective, discovered that the Dongfang Printing House at number 548, Minquan Road, was illegally printing horseracing lottery tickets and selling them in the city, in violation of the prohibition. They went to the store and confiscated ten large and small printing plates, as well as hundreds of printed and unfinished lottery tickets. The owner, Zhang Yao, was arrested and taken to the police station. Also, the related persons Dai Laowu and Sun Houcheng were apprehended. They were sent to the Simple Criminal Court of the Second Special Court. The police lawyer prosecuted them for the crime of privately issuing lottery tickets under Article 281 of the Criminal Code. After repeated interrogations by Judge Zhang Shijie, Yao confessed that Dai Laowu had entrusted her to print them, and she did not know whether they were genuine or fake. Dai confessed that someone had entrusted him to print them and then handed them over to Sun Houcheng to send them to Nanchang twice. Sun also admitted to sending them on behalf. The court ordered them to be detained and to apprehend accomplices who were still at large for a combined investigation. Yesterday, they were interrogated again. The police lawyer stated that the accomplices who were at large had not yet been apprehended and requested a preliminary judgment. Judge Zhang questioned the two defendants again, and their confessions were the same as before. He immediately pronounced judgment in court. Dai Laowu was sentenced to two months of imprisonment for mediating the sale of lottery tickets that had not been approved by the government. Sun Houcheng was sentenced to 30 days of detention for mediating the sale of lottery tickets that had not been approved by the government. The number of days of detention prior to the final judgment will be credited at a rate of two days of detention for one day of imprisonment or detention. Zhang Yao was found not guilty. The confiscated lottery ticket printing plates and other items were confiscated.

The Mint is Preparing to Start Work 161

Director Guo to Go to Beijing to Ask for Instructions Soon

A Ceremony to Be Held on New Year's Day Next Year

Since Guo Biao, the director of the Central Mint, received repeated telegram orders from Finance Minister Song Ziwen to prepare for the start of work, the internal machinery has been instructed by the engineer to repair and install separately, and is waiting for Minister Song's order to start casting. The reporter of the New Voice Society went to the factory yesterday to inquire about the latest news on the preparation of the cast, which is recorded as follows:

Guo Will Go to Beijing for Instructions: All the machinery of the factory has been repaired and installed by Guo, and notices have been posted to inform the workers to wait for the starting date. However, Guo needs to report to Minister Song in Beijing on the preparation process and ask for instructions on everything. It has now been decided to leave for Beijing in a few days, which will take about a week, and then return to Shanghai.

Starting Date Has Been Decided: Regarding the starting date, it was previously rumored to be implemented within this year. It is now heard that this news is not true. The person in charge of the factory once told the reporter that a large number of silver bars have not yet been shipped from the United States, and it is difficult to hope to start casting within this year. It has now been decided by Minister Song to hold a casting ceremony on New Year's Day next year, and officially start work on the fifth. Minister Song will personally visit the factory at that time to participate in the ceremony, etc.

Saigon-Marseilles Airmail News 163

According to the Shanghai Post Office, ordinary and registered letters (including insured mail) to Bangkok, Rangoon, Calcutta, Karachi, Dukir, Baghdad, and Bayroath can now be sent via the Saigon-Marseilles airmail route, which operates once a week (the aircraft on this air route depart from Saigon every Friday and take about 11 days en route). The airmail postage for mail to the above-mentioned areas is 22 cents, 39 cents, 72 cents, 1.30 yuan, 1.54 yuan, 1.75 yuan, 2 yuan or 2.21 yuan, depending on the destination, in addition to the ordinary international postage and registration fee. If the mail is sent via the domestic state-run airmail route within China, domestic airmail postage must be added.

Workers at Datong Bookstore Still Did Not Resume Work Yesterday 164

The Arrested Workers Have Been Fined and Released by the Court

The Company Will Recruit New Workers

Four Offices Have Issued a Declaration in Support

After the general strike of all employees of Datong Bookstore, the Party and government organs jointly issued a notice, ordering the resumption of work within three days, or it would be regarded as voluntary dismissal, and the company was allowed to recruit new workers to supplement the vacancies. Yesterday was the third day, and the employees insisted on not resuming work because the salary conditions were still not resolved. The arrested worker Xu Xinong was sentenced by the First Special District Court yesterday, fined 20 yuan and released. It is heard that the company is preparing to recruit new workers to replace the workers who refused to obey the order to resume work.

The Business, China, World, and Minzhi four offices issued a declaration in support of the Datong Bookstore workers' strike, saying: All Shanghai printing workers, under the heavy oppression of foreign imperialism and domestic capitalists, we are busy all day long, without enough food and clothing. In addition, the long-term chaos of domestic politics in recent years, exorbitant taxes, endless exploitation, soldiers, bandits, and plagues have come one after another. Our workers' lives are suffering to the point of being unbearable, and capitalists are even more recklessly exploiting their private desires, extending working hours, reducing wages, and dismissing workers. Therefore, it is impossible for us workers to maintain a minimum standard of living, so improving our lives is an urgent need for all workers in the country. The Datong Bookstore workers have been asking the capitalists to improve their treatment for several months in order to maintain their livelihoods. But the Datong Bookstore capitalists first dealt with it perfunctorily, then shirked responsibility, and now they dare to openly refuse, and threaten the workers' leaders to leave the factory, and even publicly announce that they will dismiss a large number of workers. Datong workers have no choice but to take strike action to deal with the capitalists, which is the action that Datong workers should take, and it is also the thing that all Shanghai printing workers urgently need to support. The strike has now been going on for six days, and the Datong capitalists have no sincerity to resolve the conditions, arrest workers, fabricate facts, post notices, and publish them in various newspapers to confuse public opinion and conspire to destroy the unity of the workers and deprive the workers of the benefits they deserve. Therefore, all the workers in our four offices are in the same class and share the same interests, so it is necessary to actively support them. We should use the united strength of more than 6,000 workers to fight the Datong capitalists. All Shanghai printing workers, we should know that the glorious and arduous struggle of Datong workers to improve their lives is the same as our struggle for the liberation of all printing workers. It is the first voice of our printing workers' liberation movement. Success or failure is of great importance to the future of printing workers' lives. We should all come forward to support, contribute money to help, publicize and call on, all of which are the tasks of every printing worker. The workers of our four offices will make the greatest efforts to support the Datong workers to achieve the final victory. It is hoped that all Shanghai printing workers will continue to support us and be a backing for the Datong workers. All Shanghai printing workers, hurry up and support the Datong striking workers. At the same time, it is especially hoped that all Shanghai printing workers will not be employed by the capitalists before the Datong conditions are resolved.

No. 108

The Central Bank's 108th inspection report on the issuance of currency reserve states: According to the provisions of Article 15 of the Central Bank Regulations, this committee is responsible for inspecting the reserve fund for the issuance of convertible banknotes by this bank. Today, November 20, 1931, the 108th inspection was held at the Issuing Bureau of this bank, and the results of the inspection are announced as follows: (A) The total amount of convertible banknotes issued is 35,497,075 silver dollars, including 32,814,649 silver dollar notes and 2,682,426 subsidiary currency notes. The total amount of convertible banknote reserve is 35,497,075 silver dollars, including 22,811,243 silver dollars in cash reserve. The cash reserve includes 17,056,886 yuan stored in the bank's issuing treasury, 2,117,879 yuan stored in branch banks in various ports, 3,636,478 yuan stored in the same industry, and a guarantee reserve equivalent to 12,685,832 silver dollars. (B) The total amount of customs gold convertible notes issued is 500,000 yuan. The total amount of customs gold convertible note reserve is 500,000 yuan. The reserve includes 200,000 U.S. dollars stored in the same industry in this port, with a fixed price of 40 to the customs gold as above. According to Article 2 of the Central Bank's convertible note regulations, 60% of the cash reserve and 40% of the guarantee reserve. The results of this inspection are in accordance with the regulations, with the amount of cash exceeding 60 points and the amount of guarantee less than 40 points. This report is specially made. Suichang Matches Are Indeed Domestic Products 175

The Zhejiang Lishui Suichang Match Company's factory name has one character that happens to be the same as the Japanese-owned Suisheng Match Company operating in Zhenjiang, causing the Liu Hai, Shenzhou, Ku Cang, Fisherman, etc., brand matches sold by Suichang Company in Xiamen to be mistakenly identified as Japanese goods and detained by the Xiamen Anti-Japanese National Salvation Association. This was because Xiamen is far away in southern Fujian, and the situation is unclear. Furthermore, the coincidental similarity of the "Sui" character led to the misunderstanding. Upon further investigation, all kinds of goods produced by the Suichang Match Company, except for a small number of packaging papers and chemicals like potassium chlorate and red phosphorus, which must be supplied by countries such as England, America, Germany, and Switzerland (as these few types are not produced domestically), the remaining dozen or so medicinal materials are indeed entirely domestic products, and half of them are local products of Lishui, not requiring external sourcing. In particular, the bulk raw materials such as matchbox pieces and matchsticks are supplied by the local Puchang Matchbox and Stick Factory. Therefore, the products are of excellent quality, not inferior to imported goods.

At this time when a great enemy is at our doorstep and national humiliation has not been avenged, how can partial pain affect the national patriotic movement and cause foreign countries to laugh at us? Moreover, after the announcement of the measures for disposing of Japanese goods, what methods will be used to prevent unscrupulous merchants from taking the opportunity to sell Japanese goods, and what kind of abuses will result? We ask your esteemed committee to consult and lead, and we assume that there will be no difference in the steps towards jointly facing national crisis. Therefore, we have specially sent this letter for your review, hoping that you will clearly explain the meaning of the publicly announced Announcement No. 2 to dispel public doubts. The urgency cannot be expressed fully.' etc. This letter was sent, and there should have been a receipt, so it must have reached the record room long ago, but we have not yet received a reply, which is very surprising. Therefore, we are re-extracting the original letter as follows, asking you to promptly review and reply, and please do not delay any further."

District 14: The Fourteenth District Branch of the Citizens' United Association of Edward Road held its inaugural meeting at the Tian'an Church on Shandong Road yesterday afternoon at 2:00 p.m., with more than 130 people present. The presidium included Min Caizhang, Lu Tingjian, Jiang Junyi, Zhang Baozhong, and Wu Ban-chang. The ceremony was performed according to protocol. The chairman reported on the preparations and the election results were announced. Lu Tingjian, Min Caizhang, Jiang Junyi, Qian Qun, Li Lianbo, Ji Guozhen, Qiu Pingsan, Zhang Baozhong, Lu Zhihong, Cheng Nianpeng, Cai Qinsheng, Xi Ansheng, and Zhao Zhongliang were elected as executive committee members. Wu Ban-chang, Tang Shiyi, Fan Huichun, and Zhang Peijin were elected as alternate executive committee members. A photograph was taken, and the meeting adjourned.

District 24: The Twenty-Fourth District Branch of the Citizens' United Association held its inauguration ceremony yesterday. Zhang Yichen was publicly elected as chairman. The ceremony was performed according to protocol, and a report was given. Then, an oath was taken, followed by the distribution of duties. Zhang Yichen, Shen Tianxin, and Tong Huitang were appointed as permanent members, Yu Zhongxian and Xu Jinggong were appointed as secretaries, Yang Guangxing, Zhou Hongquan, and Chen Yongzhong were appointed as general affairs, Sun Liechang and Wang Weiying were appointed for mediation, Zhang Shuliang and Zhuang Zunyan were appointed for propaganda, Wang Shaofu and Yang Guangya were appointed for organization, and Shen Tianxin, Tong Huitang, and Yang Guangxing were appointed as attending representatives. The following matters were discussed on the spot: (1) Yongshun Hardware Store reported that it had Japanese goods in stock, which it had registered in accordance with the principles of the Anti-Japanese Association, but was also accused of hiding Japanese goods, and its employees were detained and fined 5,000 yuan. It requested that fairness be advocated and assistance be provided. It was resolved to have Tong Huitang investigate whether there was a registration certificate and then verify it. (2) Yongfeng Electrical Appliance Factory reported that the copper skin it used had been detained by the Anti-Japanese Association and requested that its rights be protected. It was resolved to send a letter to the City Federation General Association for verification and forwarding to the Anti-Japanese Association for return. (3) It was proposed that the dates for the meetings of the Executive Committee and the Standing Committee should be stipulated. It was resolved that A. The Standing Committee would meet once a week; B. The Executive Committee would meet once every two weeks; C. The time and date would be 7:00 p.m. every Friday. (4) It was proposed that personnel should be assigned to be responsible for the organization of the volunteer army committee. It was resolved to appoint Zhou Hongquan, Yang Guangxing, and Tong Huitang as three committee members. The rest is omitted.

District 25: The Twenty-Fifth District Branch of the Special District Citizens' United Association held its third executive committee meeting the day before yesterday at 3:00 p.m. Chairman Zhang Bingrong presided over the meeting and conducted the ceremony according to protocol. (A) The minutes of the previous meeting were read. (B) Discussions: (1) The City Federation sent down a case in which all the tenants of Yokohama Road and Jingyun Lane requested that the landlord be prevented from oppressing them and increasing the rent. It was resolved to have Committee Member Ye Qichang and Committee Member Zhang Bingrong first investigate the facts and then handle the matter. (2) Fuli Leather Shoe Store sent a letter stating that Dr. Jiang Shangfeng used hygiene as an excuse to send a letter to the Public Security Bureau to ban them, and requesting the association to explain the matter to the Public Security Bureau. It was resolved to send separate letters to Jiang Shangfeng and the Second Precinct of the Fifth District, explaining everything. (3) Citizen Yu Xiqiao sent a letter regarding the Anti-Japanese Association's permission to sell Korean products and requested an explanation of the doubts. It was resolved to have Committee Member Chen Jiufeng explain to the citizen. (4) Wu Yulin reported that 48 volunteers had been recruited in two batches and should be examined for physical fitness separately. It was resolved to hand the matter over to the standing committee member of the Military Committee. (5) Wang Zhixiang reported that dozens of Japanese ruffians had broken into the inspection station in Zhabei today and deliberately caused trouble. The inspection station detained four Japanese on the spot, and he was afraid that it would cause disputes. It was resolved to have Ye Qichang, Hang Wujiu, Wu Yulin, Wang Zhixiang, and Yu Dongshan go to investigate. As a result, Inspector Gao Hongbin of the Fifth Precinct of the Public Security Bureau led a large team of police officers to maintain order at the scene, and fortunately no disputes occurred. The four Japanese were taken away by District Chief Wang, accompanied by two representatives from the Japanese Consulate. (6) Committee Member Wang Chengchan reported that citizens He Binglin and others on Wusong Road were planning to form a volunteer army and proposed to cooperate with the volunteer army formed by the association. It was resolved not to cooperate. (7) Wang Zhixiang reported that there are workers with legitimate occupations who are interested in joining the volunteer army. Can they be recruited? It was resolved to recruit them and asked the reporter to work hard to introduce them. (8) Committee Member Fan Peng proposed that Lin Shan, a tax collector from the Nanshi Collection Office of the Native Yellow Wine Tax Bureau, extorted 54 yuan from the Dong Zhihe store, a branch of this association, on the 15th for 54 jars of native yellow wine with special licenses for tax payment. Because the matter was illegal and resembled fraudulent deception, they refused to bribe him and sternly refused. The next day, Lin Shan led four police officers from the Third Precinct of the Fifth District and forcibly drove away 51 jars of native yellow wine. Inspector Wang issued a receipt, but the wine was nowhere to be found and was not in the Third Precinct of the Fifth District. This hinders business and causes huge losses. He requested active negotiation. It was resolved to send a letter to the Native Yellow Wine Tax Collection Office to return the wine and severely punish the illegal Lin Shan as a warning to others, and to send a letter to the Third Precinct of the Fifth District of the Public Security Bureau, asking why the wine was driven to other places after the receipt was issued, and requesting the precinct to reply as soon as possible to facilitate negotiation. The meeting adjourned at 6:30 p.m.

District 26: The Twenty-Sixth District Branch of the Citizens' United Association convened its first standing committee meeting the day before yesterday at 10:00 a.m. Chairman Wang Hanliang presided over the meeting, which was conducted according to protocol. (A) Incoming documents were reported. (B) Proposals were discussed. (1) How to advocate comforting and encouraging Ma Zhanshan, who swore to defend the country and be loyal to the border areas, to boost morale. It was resolved (A) to send a telegram of condolences, (B) to find ways to donate funds to reward the troops. (2) At the critical moment of saving the country and resisting the invaders, a plan should be expressed. It was resolved to send a telegram to the National Government to quickly determine a plan to save the country and to mobilize troops to drive out the Japanese immediately. (3) The League of Nations should uphold justice and preserve its credibility. Please impose sanctions on the violent Japanese. It was resolved to send a telegram to the Council of the League of Nations to uphold justice. (4) A volunteer army should be quickly established as a rear defense. It was resolved to submit the list of names so that they could be included in the New World Training. Other cases were discussed until 11:00 a.m., when the meeting adjourned.

District 29: The Twenty-Ninth District Branch of the Special District Citizens' United Association convened an executive committee meeting the day before yesterday at 7:00 p.m. Chairman Yu Yangsheng presided over the meeting, which was conducted according to protocol. (A) The chairman reported on the purpose of the meeting and the motions from the previous session. (B) Discussions: (1) How to comfort Chairman Ma of Heilongjiang Province, who has been loyal to the border areas. It was resolved to have Hu Yangren, Rong Zigan, Yu Yangsheng, Zhang Maosheng, Song Xiachuan, Gan Zhaocheng, and Zhu Daoquan solicit donations from all business circles. (2) To restore the national territory, mobilize to resist the invaders, and preserve the foundation of the country, a proposal should be made. It was resolved to send a telegram to Chairman Chiang of the National Government, requesting that troops be sent to resist the Japanese as soon as possible. (3) The League of Nations should fulfill the Non-Aggression Pact and preserve justice and international credibility. A joint telegram should be sent to the International Council. (4) Every man is responsible for the survival of the nation, and a volunteer army should be recruited as a rear support for the country. It was resolved to set up a registration office and notify the shops in this district to join the army for the country. (5) How to discuss the funding issues of the association. Fei Shenzhai said that there should be a budget to determine the method. It was resolved that the seven committee members would jointly handle the monthly donations. Other important cases were discussed, and the meeting adjourned.

Reader Correspondence 179

Announcement: Since October 22nd, this column has raised four questions to solicit opinions, namely (1) regarding the League of Nations, (2) regarding boycotting Japanese goods, (3) regarding volunteer army, (4) regarding uniting people's hearts to deal with foreign enemies. In the past month, many replies have been received. Those that have been published in this column include Mr. Lin Yifang, Mr. Liu Boyong, Mr. Zhongxia, and Mr. Zheng Hongsheng's opinions on boycotting Japanese goods, Mr. Qingyuan's opinion on the volunteer army, and Mr. Ding Jichan's opinion on uniting together to deal with foreign enemies, all of which have great value. In addition, there are quite a few others that could not be published due to space limitations. Now that the situation has changed drastically, the national crisis is becoming more urgent, the League of Nations negotiations have completely failed, the bitter battle in Heilongjiang has finally fallen, and the disturbances in Tianjin continue unabated. In the midst of this precarious situation for China's national destiny, mere worry, anxiety, and impatience are useless. All of us citizens should stand up, muster deep courage, and rack our brains to come up with a relatively appropriate plan for the current major issues and contribute them to the authorities and the people. Now, please raise two questions as follows: (1) Japan's trampling on Heilongjiang and invading the Middle East route not only disregards our country's sovereignty but also provokes Soviet Russia. According to common sense, Soviet Russia can no longer tolerate it. If it joins the war, it will repeat the Russo-Japanese War of 27 years ago. At that time, what attitude should our country take towards Japan and Soviet Russia? If it involves European and American countries, how should we deal with each country? (2) Chairman Chiang of the National Government has decided to set off north in the near future to recover lost territories. This is of course what the national people are eagerly looking forward to. From now on, the overall situation will change dramatically. Regarding military preparations, the government is of course responsible. On the part of the people, what responsibilities should they fulfill and what work should they do? How should boycotting Japanese goods, training volunteer army, etc., be done better? Each answer should be limited to a maximum of 1,000 words. Say less empty words and focus on methods. This newspaper will select the best ones for disclosure and public discussion based on the capacity of this column. If you agree with the methods proposed by others, please also state your opinion. Please still provide your full name, gender, age, occupation, or place of study, and native place, and attach a communication stamp and a corresponding amount of postage stamps, so that those who are not published in the newspaper can be informed by letter. As for the three questions of study, occupation, and marriage, they will still be handled according to the usual procedures. Respectfully announced.

Xing Li-jun's News 180

(Advocates donating confiscated Japanese goods for military expenses against Japan)

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce's proposed method of disposing of confiscated Japanese goods superficially protects merchants' hardships, but in reality, it eases the anti-Japanese sentiment. Currently, the violent Japanese invasion is becoming more urgent, and Heihe has been captured again. Although the League of Nations is meeting in Paris, it will definitely not be able to save China. Moreover, Japan's internal ideological problems are very serious. If it uses all its strength against us, a revolution will inevitably occur within the country. China's national spirit is now aroused and can be used. Armed recovery of the lost territories is indeed a good opportunity to save the country. However, the expenses for weapons, ammunition, and provisions are extremely high. If the confiscated Japanese goods are donated to cover military expenses, it would greatly help in recovering the lost territories. Our country does not lack generals, nor does it lack soldiers, but it lacks provisions and ammunition. The confiscated Japanese goods in Shanghai already amount to more than 20 million yuan. If more are added from other ports, it would be more than enough for two months of military expenses. Merchants love the country and do not fall behind. What do the gentlemen of the Shanghai Chamber of Commerce think?

(Answer) The method of disposing of confiscated Japanese goods has been detailed in yesterday's reply to Mr. Zhang Liyang and Mr. Li-Shi's News. Please review it.

Weather Report 182

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast for yesterday at 4:30 p.m. stated that the Yangtze River basin and coastal areas will be cloudy and colder, with occasional rainfall in some areas. A north wind is strengthening over Shandong and the Yellow Sea. The wind in the East Sea is erratic. There is a cyclone in Kyushu due to the passage of a low-pressure area moving northeast. The weather is bad east of Luzon. The center of the hurricane was within 120 miles of the intersection of 18.4 degrees north latitude and 129 degrees east longitude at 2:00 p.m., appearing to stall. Also, within the 24 hours before 3:00 p.m. yesterday, the highest temperature in Shanghai was 63.0 and the lowest was 56.3. On the same day last year, the highest was 58.5 and the lowest was 29.3.

Letter to the Editor 183

Sir, on the 20th of this month, I read in the newspaper that Feng Yongchang of the Peichang Company and broker Hua Jinzhang had violently beaten members of the Anti-Japanese Association and snatched their badges. This does not conform to the facts. Upon investigation, the members of the Anti-Japanese Association were conducting an inspection, and Mr. Feng and Mr. Hua explained the matter to them, but there was absolutely no violent beating of members or snatching of badges. Recently, because the matter involves discrepancies, we have no choice but to truthfully inform your newspaper and ask you to publish it in the "Letter to the Editor" section to clarify the truth of the day and avoid misunderstandings. We would be extremely grateful. Respectfully submitted to the chief editor of the Shenbao by Peichang Iron Company on November 21st, the Republic of China (Year 20).

Shanghai Market

Market News 185

Liangchen Haoyou Society, located at the intersection of Beijing Road and Zhejiang Road, declares that, in order to assist the anti-Japanese movement, the society has produced "Anti-Japanese Stationery," printed on Yuzhu paper, eight columns wide, 100 sheets per bag, with ten kinds of anti-Japanese illustrations, and printed on the stationery in Imitation Song typeface are the words "Compatriots quickly rise up to resist Japan and save the country." The original price is 35 cents, now reduced to 28 cents; wholesale price is only 2.5 yuan per thousand sheets. Sales start today. Many businesses and organizations have placed bulk orders for gifts and commemorative items. In addition, Zhang Zhenlu, a famous calligrapher of the society, is sacrificing his paper and ink to raise funds to support Heihe. Those who donate 10 yuan will receive a five-foot couplet, and those who donate 100 yuan will receive another piece of calligraphy of their choice. The society will handle the remittance. Mr. Zhang issued a declaration yesterday, saying, "The Japanese bandits are invading, the borderlands are falling, I grieve for my surviving compatriots, telegrams and letters are flying about, lamenting that the end is near. Alas, these great old men, although the war letters are urgent, they remain unopened. Only General Ma Zhanshan of Heilongjiang, single-handedly guarding the pass, is struggling to defend the isolated army, making a proper defense and thwarting the ferocious power of the victor. The city will fall with the man, the people's will is the general's will, which is enough to be called a good leader who protects the country and appeases the people. Is there no shame for the senior officials of the border defense command? Yinghuan admires his public service and loyalty, and national history will shine for it. Such rare talents will naturally be followed by the whole country. How can we, with the heart of a wolf, bear to watch the fire from across the river? I am a humble scholar, with a meager life of three feet, willing to relieve the difficulties, but unable to destroy the family. I can barely write official documents, and I also think of going to war and brandishing a spear, but I am powerless to tie a chicken, and in the end, I am just a scholar carrying a plan. I only think that in the icy and snowy frontier, we need food and drink, so I donate paper and ink and widely give away calligraphy couplets. All the donations received will be used for remittances. I will do my best and it does not matter if I break my arm. Wielding a brush is like a thousand-man army, and collecting small contributions will build a strong fortress. Alas, who has no ancestors, who has no wife and children, who has no descendants? We should all be quick to take the lead, and eagerly empty our pockets to protect our divine and glorious youth. People are not plants, people are not iron and stone, people are not deer and pigs. Faced with this urgent crisis, hesitating and preserving our eggs is willingly becoming a slave of a fallen nation. Let us see the unanimous support of the people's hearts and virtues, and make it a prelude to the government's dispatch of troops. How regrettable, let us arise and act!"
